### [1] [Neither Layer Alone: Epistemic Integrity Requires Hierarchical Joint Design for Long-Running AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04017v1)
*Zhihong Shen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出界面波动性是AI代理失败的新原因，并主张通过模型-工具联合设计中的显式接口契约来实现代理认知完整性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时间运行的AI代理因界面波动性（模型和工具层独立演化导致语义变化）而失败，现有架构未将代理认知完整性作为一等约束。

Method: 提出模型-工具接口契约作为联合设计的前提，定义四级层次结构（目标有效性、动作原型排序、工具实例选择、调用级故障区分）来规范边界保留内容和模型结构化输出。

Result: 将代理设计从平坦动作循环重构为契约保持的持久状态控制，评估和训练应基于契约测试信念、工具和目标承诺的保持。

Conclusion: 代理认知完整性应作为一等架构约束，通过接口契约实现，以解决界面波动性问题。

中文摘要：长时间运行的AI代理不仅在推理失败或工具指定不足时失败，而且当独立演化的模型层和工具层改变跨越它们边界的信念、能力和目标承诺的语义时也会失败——这篇论文将这类失败称为界面波动性。本文认为，代理认知完整性（AEI）必须被视为一等架构约束，只有通过围绕显式接口契约组织的联合模型-工具设计才能实现。核心主张是，模型-工具接口契约是联合设计的前提条件；其操作形式是一个四级层次结构——目标有效性、动作原型排序、工具实例选择和调用级故障区分——它规定了边界必须保留的内容以及模型必须返回的结构化输出，以使契约在各个层级上得以保持。这将长时间运行的代理设计从平坦的动作循环重新定位为对持久状态的契约保持控制。因此，评估和训练应源于契约本身，测试信念、工具和目标承诺是否在会话边界和独立层升级之间得以保持。

Original abstract: Long-running AI agents fail not only when inference fails or tools are underspecified, but when independently evolving model and harness layers change the semantics of belief, capability, and goal commitments across their boundary - a failure class this paper terms Interface Volatility. This paper argues that Agent Epistemic Integrity (AEI) must be treated as a first-class architectural constraint, achievable only through joint model-harness design organized around an explicit interface contract. The central claim is that the model-harness interface contract is the precondition for joint design; its operational form is a four-level hierarchy - goal validity, action-archetype sequencing, tool-instance selection, and invocation-level failure discrimination - that specifies what the boundary must preserve and what structured outputs the model must return for the contract to hold across levels. This reframes long-running agent design away from flat action loops and toward contract-preserving control over persistent state. Evaluation and training should therefore derive from the contract itself, testing whether belief, tool, and goal commitments hold across session boundaries and independent layer upgrades.

</details>


### [2] [Overcoming Challenges in Agile and DevOps Integration: A Qualitative Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01676v1)
*Juliana Fraislebem,Mali Senapathi,Michael Neumann,Eva-Maria Schön*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过定性方法识别了敏捷与DevOps整合的四大挑战和四大解决方案，强调文化对齐和自动化的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管敏捷和DevOps被广泛采用，但其整合面临诸多挑战，研究旨在深入理解这些挑战并提出可行解决方案。

Method: 采用半结构化访谈的定性研究方法，对巴西和德国的六位经验丰富的行业专业人士进行访谈。

Result: 识别了文化与组织障碍、结构限制、过程与方法复杂性、技术限制四类挑战；以及团队结构与自主权、文化与协作、流程与变更管理、自动化与基础设施四类解决方案。

Conclusion: 文化对齐、主动监控和自动化等实践有助于减轻整合摩擦，为软件组织提供实践指导。

中文摘要：针对日益依赖敏捷和DevOps方法论以提高软件交付速度和质量的情况，本研究调查了与它们整合相关的持续挑战和可行解决方案。尽管敏捷提倡迭代开发和客户响应性，DevOps强调自动化和运营效率，但它们在实践中融合往往带来显著的组织、结构和技术障碍。本研究采用基于对巴西和德国的六位经验丰富的行业专业人士的半结构化访谈的定性方法论，这些专业人士在敏捷和DevOps领域均有丰富经验。研究确定了整合挑战的四个核心类别：文化与组织障碍、结构限制、过程与方法复杂性以及技术限制。此外，它提供了四个主要解决方案领域：团队结构与自主权、文化与协作、流程与变更管理以及自动化与基础设施。研究结果强调了文化对齐、主动监控、自动化和其他实践在减轻整合摩擦中的重要性。结果有助于更深入理解敏捷-DevOps接口，并为寻求有效应对这一复杂转型的软件组织提供实践见解。

Original abstract: In response to the growing reliance on Agile and DevOps methodologies for enhancing software delivery speed and quality, this study investigates the persistent challenges and viable solutions associated with their integration. Although Agile promotes iterative development and customer responsiveness, and DevOps emphasizes automation and operational efficiency, their convergence in practice often presents significant organizational, structural, and technical hurdles. This research employs a qualitative methodology grounded in semi-structured interviews with six seasoned industry professionals across Brazil and Germany, each with extensive experience in both Agile and DevOps domains. The study identifies four core categories of integration challenges: Cultural & Organizational Barriers, Structural Constraints, Process \& Method Complexity, and Technical Limitations. Additionally, it offers four major solution domains: Team Structure & Autonomy, Culture & Collaboration, Process & Change Management, and Automation & Infrastructure. The findings underscore the importance of cultural alignment, proactive monitoring, automation, and other practices in mitigating integration friction. The results contribute to a deeper understanding of the Agile-DevOps interface and offer practical insights for software organizations seeking to navigate this complex transition effectively.

</details>


### [3] [Faster than the Team, Faster than the Customer: Tool Integration, Collaboration, and Organisational Lag in AI-assisted RE](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01772v2)
*Jan-Philipp Steghöfer*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过调查和访谈揭示了生成式AI在工业需求工程中的实际使用情况，发现工具集成而非能力是关键约束，且AI对团队互动的影响复杂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在需求工程中的工业实践影响尚不明确，需要实证研究。

Method: 结合2024年全公司使用案例调查和2025-2026年对八位产品负责人的两轮半结构化访谈，分析内部聊天机器人和七种商业AI工具的使用。

Result: 识别出15个用例分为四类；发现AI对PO-开发者互动影响混合，工具集成是主要约束，AI进步快于组织系统。

Conclusion: 实践已超越现有文献，从业者需关注跨工具集成、客户治理和角色边界协商。

中文摘要：将生成式人工智能工具应用于需求工程（RE）在工业实践中的影响仍然知之甚少。本文研究了在XITASO（一家中型高科技软件工程企业）中，AI辅助的需求工程工具如何在工业实践中被使用，以及它们如何重塑工作流程、工具集成和产品负责人（PO）与开发人员之间的关系。我们结合了2024年全公司范围的使用案例调查，以及2025年末和2026年春季对八位产品负责人进行的两轮半结构化访谈，涵盖了内部聊天机器人和七种商业AI工具。我们识别出15个不同的用例，分为四类：产品待办事项管理、招标管理、需求和领域理解，以及文档和工件创建。出现了三个发现。首先，AI对产品负责人与开发人员互动的影响是混合的：主流的单用户交互模式可能替代协作对话，并且开发人员并不总是欢迎AI生成的工件。其次，工具集成——而非工具能力——是约束条件：在集成到位的地方，时间节省非常显著；在集成缺失的地方，产品负责人则退回到手动变通方法。第三，AI的进步速度快于周围的组织系统，因此其好处累积到单个产品负责人身上，而团队流程和客户准备程度仍然是瓶颈。实证的GenAI-RE文献仍然以早期、实验室导向的孤立任务评估为主，而实践已经进入了尚未研究的领域：从业者已经在组合跨工具集成、应对客户治理以及重新协商角色边界。从这些模式中，我们推导出一系列问题，供考虑采用AI辅助RE的从业者根据自身情况提出。

Original abstract: The impact of applying generative AI tools to requirements engineering (RE) in industrial practice remains poorly understood. This paper examines how AI-assisted RE tools are used in industrial practice at XITASO, a medium-sized enterprise for high-tech software engineering, and how they reshape workflows, tool integration, and PO--developer relationships. We combine a 2024 company-wide use-case survey with two rounds of semi-structured interviews with eight product owners (POs) in late 2025 and spring 2026, covering an in-house chatbot and seven commercial AI tools. We identify 15 distinct use cases across four categories: product backlog management, tender management, requirements and domain understanding, and document and artifact creation. Three findings emerge. First, the effect of AI on PO--developer interaction is mixed: the prevailing single-user interaction model can substitute for collaborative dialogue, and developers do not always welcome AI-generated artefacts. Second, tool integration -- not tool capability -- is the binding constraint: where integration is in place, time savings are dramatic; where it is missing, POs fall back on manual workarounds. Third, AI advances faster than the surrounding organisational systems, so its benefits accrue to individual POs while team processes and customer readiness remain the bottleneck. The empirical GenAI-RE literature remains dominated by early-stage, lab-oriented evaluations of isolated tasks while practice has moved into territory it has not yet studied: practitioners are already assembling cross-tool integrations, navigating customer governance, and renegotiating role boundaries. From these patterns we derive a set of questions practitioners considering AI-assisted RE may ask of their own situation.

</details>


### [4] [Improving LLM-Based Go Code Review through Issue-List Generation and Context Augmentation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01859v1)
*Kexin Sun,Yucong Guan,Jiaqi Sun,Hongyu Kuang,Guoping Rong,Dong Shao,He Zhang,Xiaoxing Ma,Christoph Treude*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过问题列表审查和上下文增强，LLM代码审查的性能显著提升，最佳配置达到28.00%精化精确匹配，接近人类上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 改进LLM代码审查的生成策略和上下文增强以提高其实际效用，因为现有方法依赖单一问题报告且缺乏有效的上下文利用。

Method: 提出问题列表审查范式；比较相邻、基于LSP的语义和基于IR的相似协同变更三种上下文增强；整合无上下文和上下文增强候选列表；引入精化引导剪枝控制候选数量。

Result: 最佳配置（问题列表审查+相邻和相似协同变更上下文+候选整合）达到28.00%精化精确匹配，比无上下文主问题审查（17.15%）提高10.85个百分点，优于CodeReviewer（15.02%），接近人类上限（36.09%）；精化引导剪枝将平均候选数从7.2降至3.1（top-5）且几乎不损失性能。

Conclusion: 结合问题列表审查、上下文增强和候选整合可大幅提升LLM代码审查效果，精化引导剪枝在保持性能的同时减少候选数量，使结果更实用。

中文摘要：LLMs在自动化代码审查方面展现出巨大潜力，但其实际效用严重依赖于生成和上下文策略的设计。在本文中，我们研究如何通过生成策略和上下文增强来改进基于LLM的代码审查。我们首先提出了一种问题列表审查范式，其中LLM枚举所有潜在问题，而不是仅报告最重要的问题（即主问题审查）。然后，我们系统地比较了三种类型的代码上下文增强——相邻上下文、基于LSP的语义上下文和基于IR的相似协同变更上下文——并研究它们如何影响问题发现。最后，我们整合了无上下文和上下文增强生成的候选列表，以提高审查覆盖率，并引入了精化引导剪枝以将候选列表保持在实用规模。我们在1,438个Go审查实例上评估了我们的方法，使用下游代码精化作为主要指标，即候选列表至少包含一条与最终人工修订相同代码变更的评论的频率。为了比较，我们在相同的基于精化的评估下评估了CodeReviewer（一个专门为审查评论生成训练的模型）的评论，以及真实人类审查评论（作为实际上限）。结果表明，我们最佳配置结合了问题列表审查、相邻和相似协同变更上下文以及候选整合，达到了28.00%的精化精确匹配，比没有任何额外上下文的主问题审查（17.15%）显著提高了+10.85个百分点，大幅优于CodeReviewer（15.02%），并接近人类专家上限36.09%。我们的精化引导剪枝将平均候选数量从7.2减少到3.1（前5个），同时几乎保留了全部效益，使候选列表更易于检查。

Original abstract: LLMs have shown strong potential for automating code review, yet their practical utility depends heavily on the design of generation and context strategies. In this paper, we investigate how to improve LLM-based code review through generation strategy and contextual augmentation. We first propose an issue-list review paradigm, in which LLMs enumerate all potential issues rather than reporting only the single most important one (i.e., primary-issue review). We then systematically compare three types of code context augmentation -- neighboring, LSP-based semantics, and IR-based similar co-change context -- and study how they influence issue discovery. Finally, we integrate candidates from no-context and context-enhanced generation to improve review coverage, and introduce refinement-guided pruning to keep the candidate list at a practical size. We evaluate our approach on 1,438 Go review instances using downstream code refinement as the main metric, i.e., how often the candidate list contains at least one comment inducing the same code change as the final human revision. For comparison, we evaluate comments by CodeReviewer, a model trained specifically for review comment generation, as well as ground-truth human review comments (as a practical upper bound), under the same refinement-based evaluation. The results show that our best configuration, combining issue-list review, neighboring and similar co-change context, and candidate integration, reaches 28.00% refinement exact match, a statistically significant gain of +10.85 percentage points over primary-issue review without any additional context (17.15%), substantially outperforming CodeReviewer (15.02%) and approaching the human-oracle ceiling of 36.09%. Our refinement-guided pruning reduces the average candidate count from 7.2 to 3.1 at top-5 while retaining nearly the full benefit, making the candidate list easier to inspect.

</details>


### [5] [Comparing ML-Specific and General Python Code Smells Across Project Characteristics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01882v1)
*Halimeh Agh,Betül Cimendag,Stefan Wagner*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过分析279个GitHub开源ML项目，发现ML专用代码异味比通用Python异味少41-94倍，且主要与提交频率和领域相关，而通用异味与项目特征无关，表明需要针对特定领域的质量策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对ML专用代码异味与项目特征关系的理解，导致质量保证策略一刀切，无法考虑上下文因素驱动的技术债务。

Method: 使用CodeSmile和Pylint工具，对279个GitHub开源ML项目进行实证分析，考察项目规模、年龄、贡献者、提交频率、CI/CD采用和领域与ML专用及通用Python代码质量的关系。

Result: （1）ML代码异味比通用Python异味少41-94倍；（2）提交频率和领域与ML专用质量显著相关，而其他特征不相关；（3）通用Python异味与任何项目特征无关；（4）受ML专用异味影响的领域与受通用异味影响的领域不同。

Conclusion: ML代码质量依赖于领域特定实践和专门的CI/CD质量门，标准自动化无法覆盖领域特定的正确性问题，需要针对异味类型定制质量策略。

中文摘要：机器学习系统由通用代码和机器学习专用代码组成。尽管已经识别出ML专用代码的代码异味，但它们与项目特征的关系以及它们与整体代码质量的相互作用尚未被充分理解。如果没有这些知识，质量保证策略仍然是一刀切的，未能考虑导致ML系统技术债务的上下文因素。我们通过检查六个项目特征（规模、年龄、贡献者、提交频率、CI/CD采用和领域）如何与279个GitHub上的开源ML项目中的ML专用和通用Python代码质量相关，提供了实证证据。使用CodeSmile检测ML代码异味和Pylint检测通用Python异味，我们的结果表明：（1）ML代码异味比通用Python异味少41-94倍；（2）提交频率和领域与ML专用质量显著相关，而项目规模、团队规模、年龄和CI/CD采用则没有，这挑战了关于技术债务的传统观点；（3）通用Python异味与任何项目特征均无关联，表明系统性的编码问题独立于项目背景；（4）受ML专用异味影响最严重的领域不一定是受通用Python异味影响最严重的领域，因此需要针对每种异味类型量身定制的质量策略。MLOps经常涉及配置问题，强化学习面临张量操作的挑战，计算机视觉遇到GPU工作流的问题。总体而言，ML代码质量取决于特定领域的实践和专门的CI/CD质量门，因为标准自动化常常忽略特定领域的正确性问题。

Original abstract: Machine learning systems consist of general-purpose code as well as machine-learning-specific code. While ML-specific code smells have been identified, their connection to project characteristics and their interaction with overall code quality are not well understood. Without this knowledge, quality assurance strategies remain one-size-fits-all, failing to account for the contextual factors that drive technical debt in ML systems. We present empirical evidence by examining how six project features (size, age, contributors, commit frequency, CI/CD adoption, and domain) relate to both ML-specific and general Python code quality in 279 open-source ML projects on GitHub. Using CodeSmile for ML code smells and Pylint for general Python smells, our results show: (1) ML code smells are 41-94 times less frequent than general Python smells; (2) commit frequency and domain are significantly associated with ML-specific quality, while project size, team size, age, and CI/CD adoption are not, challenging traditional views on technical debt; (3) general Python smells are not linked to any project characteristic, indicating systemic coding issues that are independent of project context; (4) domains that suffer most from ML-specific smells are not necessarily the same domains that suffer most from general Python smells, necessitating tailored quality strategies for each smell type. MLOps often involves configuration issues, Reinforcement Learning faces challenges with tensor manipulation, and Computer Vision encounters problems with GPU workflows. Overall, ML code quality depends on domain-specific practices and specialized CI/CD quality gates, as standard automation often overlooks domain-specific correctness problems.

</details>


### [6] [Trust-Calibrated Code Review: A Participatory Design Study of Review Workflows for LLM-Generated Multi-File Changes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01969v1)
*Lo Gullstrand Heander,Agnia Sergeyuk,Ilya Zakharov,Emma Söderberg,Nikita Mukhortov*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过参与式设计发现，审查LLM生成的多文件代码的核心挑战是信任校准，并提出了三级工作流和七个设计构件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具不支持LLM生成的多文件代码变更审查的工作流和设计，缺乏经过验证的端到端工作流或IDE工具设计。

Method: 与JetBrains合作，采用双钻石设计流程的参与式设计研究，包括发现（N=17）、定义、开发（7人返回）、交付（概念设计和原型，43人评估）阶段。

Result: 参与者将信任校准确定为核心挑战；提出三级工作流（概览、文件分析、代码片段审查）和七个设计构件（块、每行风险、每文件风险、评判者、演练、缩放、安全笼）；验证调查中所有工作流级别评分高于中性中点，63%受访者预期总体审查工作量减少，52%预期信任评估工作量减少。

Conclusion: 审查LLM生成的多文件变更本质是信任校准问题，而非差异比较问题；提出的三级工作流和七个设计构件为AI代码审查工具设计提供了概念框架。

中文摘要：背景：开发者越来越多地审查由基于LLM的代理生成的多文件代码变更，但目前尚无针对此场景的经过验证的端到端工作流或IDE工具设计。
目标：我们研究（RQ1）开发者在审查LLM生成的多文件变更时面临的挑战，以及（RQ2）开发者如何设想针对此任务的有效工作流。
方法：与JetBrains合作，我们采用双钻石设计流程，包括发现、定义、开发和交付阶段，进行了一项参与式设计研究。行业从业者参与了发现阶段（N=17）；其中7人返回参与开发阶段。定义阶段由作者主导综合。交付阶段产生了一个概念设计和一个高保真半交互式原型，并通过后续调查（N=43名从业者）进行了评估。
结果：参与者将信任校准确定为核心挑战。研究得出一个三级审查工作流（概览、文件分析、代码片段审查），并由七个设计构件（块、每行风险、每文件风险、评判者、演练、缩放、安全笼）支持。在验证调查中，所有三个工作流级别的评分均高于中性中点（李克特五点量表均值3.50-3.91）。63%的受访者预期总体审查工作量减少，52%预期信任评估工作量减少，相对于他们当前使用的工具。这些发现表明，设计构件为未来工具开发指明了积极方向。
结论：审查LLM生成的多文件变更是一个信任校准问题，而非差异比较问题。我们报告的三级工作流和七个设计构件为工具设计师提供了一个概念框架，用于构建AI就绪的代码审查工具，能够以开发者注意力分配的粒度展现风险和置信信号。

Original abstract: Background: Developers increasingly review multi-file code changes generated by LLM-based agents, yet no validated end-to-end workflow or IDE tooling design exists for this scenario.
  Aims: We investigate (RQ1) the challenges developers face when reviewing LLM-generated multi-file changes and (RQ2) how developers envision effective workflows for this task.
  Method: In collaboration with JetBrains, we conducted a participatory design study structured using the double-diamond design process with Discover, Define, Develop, and Deliver phases. Industry practitioners participated in the Discover phase (N=17); seven of these returned for the Develop phase. The Define phase was an author-led synthesis. The Deliver phase produced a conceptual design and a high-fidelity semi-interactive prototype evaluated through a follow-up survey with N=43 practitioners.
  Results: Participants identified trust-calibration as the central challenge. The study yielded a three-level review workflow (overview, file-analysis, code snippet review) supported by seven design constructs (chunk, risk-per-line, risk-per-file, judge, walk-through, zooming in/out, and security cage). In the validation survey, all three workflow levels scored above the neutral midpoint (means 3.50--3.91 on a five-point scale). Of the respondents, 63% expected reduced overall review effort, and 52% reduced trust-assessment effort, relative to their current tools. These findings suggest that the design constructs indicate a positive direction for future tool development.
  Conclusions: Reviewing LLM-generated multi-file changes is a trust-calibration problem rather than a diffing problem. The three-level workflow and the seven constructs we report give tool designers a conceptual framework for building AI-ready code review tools that surface risk and confidence signals at the granularity at which developers allocate attention.

### [7] [An Agentic Approach Towards Replication Package Quality Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02006v1)
*Maximilian Alexander Amougou Mbida,Florian Angermeir*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了一个多智能体方法，通过将开放科学指南转化为机器可验证的标准来自动评估复现包质量，初步评估显示高一致性和正确性，但定性研究表现不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工制品评估在经验软件工程中 largely manual and difficult to scale，需要自动化方法以支持复现性。

Method: 整合380项需求为51个可复现性标准，操作化31个用于自动化评估，实现多智能体原型系统。

Result: 在五个复现包上，运行间一致性91.4%，正确性75.4%；结构化标准表现好，定性研究表现差；试点调查显示有用性但存在认知负荷。

Conclusion: 智能体研究人工制品评估有潜力通过自动化常规检查支持作者和审稿人。

中文摘要：经验软件工程中的可复现性依赖于完整、可访问和可重用的研究人工制品，然而人工制品评估在很大程度上仍然是手动的且难以扩展。这篇新兴结果论文探索了一种智能体方法，通过将开放科学指南转化为机器可验证的标准来评估复现包质量。我们整合了来自34个来源的380项需求，形成51个可复现性标准，其中31个被操作化用于基于人工制品的自动化评估。基于这些标准，我们实现了一个多智能体原型，自动检查复现包并生成基于证据的改进报告。在五个复现包上的初步评估显示，通过与手动基准的微平均一致性，实现了91.4%的高运行间一致性和75.4%的正确性。该智能体在结构化标准（如代码、环境和人工制品可用性）上表现最佳，但在定性或混合方法研究上表现不佳。一项针对七位软件工程研究者的试点调查表明，感知有用性和采用潜力良好，同时揭示了人在回路规划步骤中的认知负荷。总体而言，这些初步结果表明，智能体研究人工制品评估有潜力通过自动化选定的常规检查来支持作者和审稿人。

Original abstract: Reproducibility in empirical software engineering relies on complete, accessible, and reusable research artifacts, yet artifact evaluation remains largely manual and difficult to scale. This emerging results paper explores an agentic approach for assessing replication package quality by translating open-science guidelines into machine-verifiable criteria. We consolidate 380 requirements from 34 sources into 51 reproducibility criteria, of which 31 are operationalized for automated artifact-based evaluation. Based on these criteria, we implement a multi-agent prototype that automatically inspects replication packages and produces evidence-grounded improvement reports. A preliminary evaluation on five replication packages shows high inter-run consistency of 91.4\% and 75.4\% correctness, through micro-averaged agreement with a manual baseline. The agent performs best on structural criteria such as code, environment, and artifact availability, but struggles with qualitative or mixed-method studies. A pilot survey with seven software engineering researchers indicates well perceived usefulness and adoption potential, while revealing cognitive load in the human-in-the-loop planning step. Overall, these emerging results indicate that agentic research artifact evaluation has the potential to support authors and reviewers by automating selected routine checks.

### [8] [CodegenBench: Can LLMs Write Efficient Code Across Architectures?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04023v1)
*Jie Li,Wenzhao Wu,Junqi Hu,Qinrui Zheng,Bowen Wu,Juepeng Zheng,Yutong Lu,Haohuan Fu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出CodegenBench基准测试，评估LLMs在三种CPU架构上的并行代码生成能力，发现其在跨平台泛化上存在局限，对中等难度问题效果较好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对LLMs在CPU导向的高性能计算跨多种架构（如申威、鲲鹏）上的代码生成能力评估，因此需要填补这一空白。

Method: 构建CodegenBench基准测试，包含106个标准BLAS例程和20个针对申威与鲲鹏架构的专业计算核心，在x86_64、申威和鲲鹏三个平台上评估LLMs的并行代码生成性能。

Result: LLMs在x86_64上能生成优化代码，但在申威和鲲鹏等特定领域架构上性能显著下降；且对实现长度短、复杂度中等的任务最有效。

Conclusion: 开源数据集和自动评估基础设施，促进LLM驱动的高性能代码生成研究，同时揭示当前LLMs在跨平台泛化上的关键局限性。

中文摘要：尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在通用编程和GPU加速环境（如PyTorch、CUDA）的代码生成任务上已被广泛评估，但它们在面向CPU的高性能计算（HPC）中跨多种架构的能力仍未得到充分探索。为填补这一空白，我们引入了CodegenBench，一个全面的基准测试套件，旨在评估跨三个不同硬件平台（x86_64、申威和鲲鹏）的高效并行代码生成。我们的基准测试包含106个标准基本线性代数子程序（BLAS）例程作为基本基线，以及20个针对每种独特超级计算架构（LeetSunway和LeetKunpeng）适配的专业计算核心。我们的广泛评估表明，尽管最先进的LLMs能够为像x86_64这样普遍存在的架构生成优化代码，但在公共文档和训练数据有限的特定领域架构上，它们表现出显著的性能下降，凸显了跨平台泛化的关键局限性。此外，我们对影响代码质量的因素（如实现长度和任务复杂度）的分析表明，当前LLMs在需要简洁代码片段的中等难度问题上最为有效。我们开源了我们的数据集和自动评估基础设施，以促进LLM驱动的高性能代码生成的未来研究。资源可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/CodegenBench-EDE1/ 和 https://anonymous.4open.science/r/CodegenBenchDataset-2551 获取。

Original abstract: While large language models (LLMs) have been extensively evaluated on code generation tasks for general-purpose programming and GPU-accelerated environments (e.g., PyTorch, CUDA), their capabilities in CPU-oriented high-performance computing (HPC) across diverse architectures remain underexplored. To bridge this gap, we introduce CodegenBench, a comprehensive benchmark suite designed to evaluate the generation of efficient parallel code across three distinct hardware platforms: x86_64, Sunway, and Kunpeng. Our benchmark comprises 106 standard Basic Linear Algebra Subprograms (BLAS) routines establishing a fundamental baseline, alongside 20 specialized computational kernels adapted for each of the unique supercomputing architectures (LeetSunway and LeetKunpeng). Our extensive evaluation reveals that while state-of-the-art LLMs can generate optimized code for ubiquitous architectures like x86_64, they exhibit significant performance degradation on domain-specific architectures with limited public documentation and training data, highlighting critical limitations in cross-platform generalization. Furthermore, our analysis of factors influencing code quality such as implementation length and task complexity indicates that current LLMs are most effective for moderately difficult problems requiring concise code snippets. We open-source our dataset and automated evaluation infrastructure to facilitate future research in LLM-driven high-performance code generation. The resources are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/CodegenBench-EDE1/ and https://anonymous.4open.science/r/CodegenBenchDataset-2551.

</details>


### [9] [Poking Around in the Dark: Why a Shared Understanding of Components Matters](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02442v1)
*Felix Reichmann,Wolfgang Krane,Alena Naiakshina,Martin Johns,Simon Koch*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文质疑SBOM依赖的组件共识假设，通过分析组件包含机制并评估五款主流SBOM生成工具，发现存在共同盲点，无法达到安全级别的SBOM，需要重新定义组件并改进工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前SBOM旨在提升软件供应链安全，但作者质疑其底层假设（组件共识和工具能力）是否成立，并希望通过实证研究揭示问题。

Method: 提出组件包含机制（CIM）分析框架，系统评估五款SBOM生成工具（cdxgen、syft、trivy、ORT、Microsoft sbom-tool），使用Python、Java、Go、PHP、Rust、C六种语言的真实数据构建基准进行测试。

Result: 没有工具覆盖所有CIM，工具间存在共同差距；SBOM在组件定义和识别上存在模糊性和盲点，无法实现安全级保障。

Conclusion: 当前SBOM工具不足以保障软件供应链安全，必须重新定义组件范围并修订生成工具，否则任何基于SBOM的安全努力都将失败。

中文摘要：通过列出应用程序中包括的组件，软件物料清单（SBOM）旨在支持及时识别易受攻击的组件并确保软件供应链的安全。然而，我们质疑一个基本假设，即对于SBOM中应列出的组件存在共识，并且当前技术足以保障软件供应链的安全。
首先，我们提出了对软件开发生命周期中组件包含机制（CIM）的基础分析。然后我们系统地分析了四种流行的SBOM生成工具：cdxgen、syft、trivy、ORT以及Microsoft的sbom-tool，以了解它们如何定义和识别相关组件。最后，我们使用跨编程语言Python、Java、Go、PHP、Rust和C的真实数据来评估这些工具。
尽管当今的工具是识别组件的一步，但我们的结果表明，没有工具覆盖所有已识别的CIM，并且工具之间存在共同的差距。我们证明，在当前模糊的定义和工具下，SBOM在组件包含方面表现出模糊性和盲点。因此，使用所评估的工具无法实现安全级别的SBOM，需要进一步进展以确保软件供应链安全。我们需要回到绘图板，澄清哪些组件应该包含在SBOM中，并相应修订SBOM生成器。没有对组件是什么的共享理解，用SBOM保障软件供应链安全的任何努力都将失败。

Original abstract: By listing the components included in an application, Software Bills of Materials (SBOMs) are intended to support the timely identification of vulnerable components and ensure the security of the software supply chain. However, we question the underlying assumption that there is agreement on the components to be listed in an SBOM and that current technology is sufficient to secure the software supply chain.
  First, we propose a ground-up analysis of Component Inclusion Mechanisms (CIM) in the software's development lifecycle. Then we systematically analyze the four popular SBOM generation tools, cdxgen, syft, trivy, ORT, and the Microsoft sbom-tool, to understand how they define and identify relevant components. Finally, we assess these using a ground truth across the programming languages Python, Java, Go, PHP, Rust, and C.
  While today's tools are a step toward identifying components, our results show that no tool covers all identified CIMs and that common gaps exist across tools. We demonstrate that, under the current vague definitions and tooling, SBOMs exhibit ambiguity and blind spots in component inclusion. Thus, a security-grade SBOM is not achievable with the evaluated tools, necessitating further progress to ensure software supply chain security. We need to go back to the drawing board to clarify which components should be included in an SBOM and revise SBOM generators accordingly. Without a shared understanding of what a component is, any effort to secure software supply chains with SBOMs will fail.

### [10] [The Biomimetic Architecture of Software 4.0](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04025v1)
*Philip Sheldrake,Dirk Scheffler*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出Software 4.0范式和Recognitive语言，通过将结构验证卸载到确定性基板，解决概率-符号阻抗不匹配，使连接主义计算转化为深度语义探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当代编程范式因历史路径依赖而无法有效承载连接主义智能，导致概率-符号阻抗不匹配和静态代码组装的高成本，现有Software 3.x方法仅增加复杂性。

Method: 引入Software 4.0自创生异质结构，包括人类智能、神经AI和反射性符号基质；提出Recognitive编程语言和平台，通过确定性基板卸载结构验证，实现软件自我调节与演化。

Result: 解锁了优越的推理时扩展机制，连接主义计算从概率模拟结构约束转向深度语义探索和假设遍历，降低了计算和财务成本。

Conclusion: 这是一篇基础性愿景论文，为连接主义意图提供理论基础，经验评估和形式规范留待未来工作。

中文摘要：主导编程范式继承了一种为单个人类思维指导本地机器的过去时代优化的执行模型，使得当代系统背负着历史路径依赖。当被迫承载多维连接主义智能时，这种脆弱的组装模型在深度的概率-符号阻抗不匹配下破裂。尽管当代Software 3.x框架试图通过将大型语言模型（LLM）封装在日益复杂的外部支架中来修补不匹配，但这种不断升级的架构复杂性只会增加静态代码组装的实际成本。为了解决原因而非效果，本文引入了Software 4.0——一种人类智能、神经AI和原生反射性符号基质的自创生异质结构。在该范式下，软件从待解析的惰性语料转变为自我调节的代谢网络，原生地验证、修改和演化自身的结构完整性。我们提出了Recognitive，即实现此架构的编程语言和平台。通过将结构验证的负担卸载到确定性基板上，它解锁了一种优越的推理时扩展机制——其中连接主义计算完全转化为深度语义探索和假设遍历，而不是以概率方式模拟结构约束的毁灭性计算和财务成本。超越传统的“软件工厂”思维，我们概述了所需的理论基础，以接地连接主义意图，并完全进入智能时代。这是一篇基础性的愿景论文；类型系统和操作语义的经验评估和形式化规范是未来工作的主题。

Original abstract: Dominant programming paradigms inherit an execution model optimised for a bygone era of a single human mind instructing a local machine, leaving contemporary systems burdened with historical path dependencies. When forced to host multi-dimensional, connectionist intelligence, this brittle assembly model fractures under the weight of a profound probabilistic-symbolic impedance mismatch. While contemporary Software 3.x frameworks attempt to patch the mismatch by encasing large language models (LLMs) in increasingly complicated external harnesses, this spiralling architectural complexity only compounds the carrying cost of static code assembly. To address the cause rather than the effects, this paper introduces Software 4.0 -- an autopoietic heterarchy of human intelligence, neural AI, and natively reflective symbolic substrate. Under this paradigm, software is transformed from an inert corpus to be parsed into a self-regulating metabolic network that natively verifies, modifies, and evolves its own structural integrity. We present Recognitive, the programming language and platform that materialises this architecture. By offloading the burden of structural verification to a deterministic substrate, it unlocks a superior inference-time scaling regime -- one where connectionist compute translates entirely into deep semantic exploration and hypothesis traversal rather than the ruinous computational and financial cost of simulating structural constraints probabilistically. Moving beyond the legacy 'Software Factory' mindset, we outline the theoretical foundations required to ground connectionist intent and arrive fully in the intelligence age. This is a foundational vision paper; empirical evaluation and formal specification of the type system and operational semantics are the subject of future work.

### [11] [Monitoring Agentic Systems Before They're Reliable](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02494v1)
*Marisa Ferrara Boston,Glen Hanson,Effi Georgala,JD Hudgens,Heather Frase*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 代理系统生产中的结构缺陷主导故障，提出三维度三范围监控方法，实验表明监控范围决定故障类型，结构缺陷掩盖任务级错误，97%发现可自动跟踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 进入生产环境的代理系统中结构缺陷主导故障，任务级错误检测因结构缺陷掩盖而不可行，需要新的监控和分类方法。

Method: 将代理系统评估分解为质量、适用性、效率三个维度，以及运行内、跨运行、结构三个监控范围，使用方差作为表征信号，并采用FMEA改编的严重性分类进行路由。

Result: 监控范围决定故障类型：运行内监控发现确定性阶段缺陷，跨运行监控发现随机集成后果，结构监控发现集成缺口；注入的任务级错误与基线无法区分；97%的发现可自动路由。

Conclusion: 提出成熟度阶段模型，监控应从结构表征过渡到错误检测再到可靠性跟踪；尽早部署监控可发现最重要问题；方法可迁移到受监管行业。

中文摘要：进入生产环境的代理系统通常以部分集成的装配体形式运行，其中结构缺陷（而非任务级错误）主导着故障格局。在这种成熟度水平下，任务级错误检测可能不可行：结构故障模式掩盖了任务级监控器设计用于检测的信号。我们提出一种监控和分类方法，将代理系统评估分解为三个维度（质量、适用性、效率）和三个监控范围（运行内、跨运行、结构），使用方差作为表征信号。发现结果通过改编自FMEA的严重性分类进行路由，将人工注意力集中到值得调查的子集上。我们在一个包含120个文档包、220次运行且注入控制错误的合成测试平台上进行评估。三个结果浮现：监控范围决定故障类型——运行内监控器发现确定性阶段缺陷（CV=0.02），跨运行监控器发现随机集成后果（CV=1.25，24%属于L2），结构监控器以完美一致性（CV=0.00）识别出集成缺口。注入的任务级错误与干净基线无法区分，证实结构缺陷掩盖了任务级信号。确定性分类将97%的发现路由到自动跟踪，留下反映可变行为的2%供人工调查。基于第一阶段证据，我们提出一个成熟度阶段模型，其中随着集成缺陷的解决，监控从结构表征过渡到错误检测再到可靠性跟踪。该分类法、基于CV的范围表征和严重性模型在架构上可迁移到受监管行业中文档驱动的多阶段代理工作流；具体校准因领域而异。尽早部署监控：它首先发现的就是最重要的待修复事项。

Original abstract: Agentic systems entering production typically operate as partially integrated assemblies where structural defects, not task-level errors, dominate the failure landscape. At this maturity level, task-level error detection may be infeasible: structural failure modes mask the signal that task-level monitors are designed to detect.We present a monitoring and triage methodology that decomposes agentic system evaluation into three dimensions (quality, suitability, efficiency) at three monitoring scopes (within-run, cross-run, structural), using variance as a characterization signal. Findings are routed through severity classification adapted from FMEA, concentrating human attention on the subset that warrants investigation. We evaluate on a synthetic testbed of 220 runs across 120 document bundles with controlled error injection.Three results emerge. Monitor scope determines failure type: within-run monitors surface deterministic stage defects (CV = 0.02), cross-run monitors surface stochastic integration consequences (CV = 1.25, 24% at L2), and a structural monitor identifies an integration gap with perfect consistency (CV = 0.00). Injected task-level errors are indistinguishable from clean baselines, confirming structural defects mask task-level signal. Deterministic triage routes 97% of findings to automated tracking, leaving the 2% reflecting variable behavior for human investigation.We propose, on Stage 1 evidence, a maturity-staging model in which monitoring transitions from structural characterization to error detection to reliability tracking as integration defects resolve. The taxonomy, CV-based scope characterization, and severity model transfer architecturally to document-driven, multi-stage agentic workflows in regulated industries; specific calibrations are domain-specific. Deploy monitoring early: the first thing it finds is the most important thing to fix.

</details>


### [12] [Acceptance-Test-Driven Evaluation Protocols for Business-Centric LLM Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02755v1)
*Eric Liang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于验收测试驱动开发的LLM系统评估协议扩展，采用红-训练-绿生命周期，将利益相关者目标转化为可执行契约和门控，确保系统满足安全、可靠、可审计和经济性要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM应用依赖概率组件却需满足确定性机构要求，普通后验基准测试不足以保障系统的安全、可靠、可审计和经济性，因此需要更严格的评估协议。

Method: 扩展评估协议，基于验收测试驱动开发、安全工程和业务验证，定义可执行行为契约、发布门控、监控信号和证据工件，并引入红-训练-绿生命周期（定义失败测试→改进系统→满足门控后发布）。

Result: 贡献了一个面向治理的度量堆栈、参考架构和实证协议，用于对比验收测试驱动开发与传统的提示词优先及后基准测试工作流程。

Conclusion: 该协议为LLM系统提供系统化的开发与评估方法，确保系统在满足机构要求的同时保持概率组件的灵活性，并通过实证对比验证其有效性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）应用日益需要在依赖概率生成组件的同时满足确定性的机构要求。这种不匹配使得普通的后验基准测试对于必须安全、可靠、可审计且经济有用的系统来说是不够的。本文贡献了一种基于验收测试驱动开发、安全工程和以业务为中心的验证的操作性LLM系统的评估协议扩展。该扩展在提示词、模型、检索或代理变更被接受之前，将利益相关者的目标转化为可执行的行为契约、发布门控、监控信号和证据工件。它将测试驱动开发的红-绿-重构纪律调整为红-训练-绿生命周期：首先定义期望行为的失败验收测试，然后通过提示词更改、检索设计、微调、护栏或数据增强来改进LLM系统，最后在满足多维门控后才发布。贡献在于一个面向治理的度量堆栈、参考架构和实证协议，用于比较验收测试驱动的LLM开发与先提示词和后基准测试工作流程。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) applications are increasingly expected to satisfy deterministic institutional requirements while relying on probabilistic generative components. This mismatch makes ordinary post-hoc benchmarking insufficient for systems that must be safe, reliable, auditable, and economically useful. This paper contributes an evaluation-protocol extension for operational LLM systems grounded in acceptance-test-driven development, safety engineering, and business-centric validation. The extension translates stakeholder goals into executable behavioral contracts, release gates, monitoring signals, and evidence artifacts before prompt, model, retrieval, or agent changes are accepted. It adapts the red-green-refactor discipline of test-driven development to a red-train-green lifecycle: first define failing acceptance tests for desired behavior, then improve the LLM system through prompt changes, retrieval design, fine-tuning, guardrails, or data augmentation, and finally release only when multidimensional gates are satisfied. The contribution is a governance-oriented metric stack, reference architecture, and empirical protocol for comparing acceptance-test-driven LLM development against prompt-first and benchmark-after workflows.

</details>


### [13] [Report on the Designing Accountable Software Systems Workshop](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02804v1)
*Catherine Albiston,Travis Breaux,Kat Dearstyne,Jane Cleland-Huang,Serge Egelman,Joan Feigenbaum,Lu Feng,Max Lindquist,Stephen Miner,Ruzica Piskac,Sarah Santos,Jordan Schmerge,Anmol Singhal,Maria Smith,Daniel Weitzner,Christopher Yoo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研讨会指出软件系统问责制需要明确定义与责任，并强调跨学科合作的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了汇集政府、学术界和工业界的利益相关者，共同探讨软件系统中问责制的跨学科问题，并系统化当前知识，明确研究空白。

Method: 通过小组讨论、特邀演讲和分组会议，涵盖问责制的多个维度，以协作知识系统化的方式进行。

Result: 明确了定义和责任的重要性；指出需要改进问责制向软件设计过程的转化；发现跨学科团队面临高要求。

Conclusion: 研讨会确定了若干研究方向，强调跨学科合作和利益相关者参与对于实现软件系统问责制的关键作用。

中文摘要：设计可问责软件系统研讨会（DASS）于2024年11月召开，得到美国国家科学基金会的支持，旨在吸引来自政府、学术界和工业界的广泛当前及未来利益相关者，共同探讨软件系统中问责制的跨学科主题。在为期两天的会议中，与会者参与了一系列小组讨论、特邀演讲和分组会议，内容涵盖：（1）问责制的维度，包括法律合规以及商业和社会方面的因素与驱动因素；（2）实现问责所需的各种结构的概念模型；（3）影响软件的法律要求来源；（4）法律要求在软件中的操作性实现；（5）保存证据以进行调查的要求；以及（6）软件之外影响问责结构成功或失败的一系列挑战和背景因素。此次研讨会以协作知识系统化的方式进行，最终确定了若干研究方向。研究结果包括澄清问责组织内定义和责任的重要性，这可能会影响问责制研究人员是否做出限制研究发现可推广性的假设。此外，还确定了需要进一步研究的方法，以改进问责制结构向软件设计过程的转化，同时改善与立法者、监管者、企业高管和系统开发者等利益相关者的互动。最后，一个关键发现是，类似DASS的研究项目对跨学科团队提出了高要求：既包括团队组建和维持方面，也包括涵盖研究方法、研究传播和职业发展的跨学科学习的特定需求。

Original abstract: The Workshop on Designing Accountable Software Systems (DASS) was convened in November 2024 with support from the U.S. National Science Foundation to engage a wide range of current and future stakeholders from government, academia, and industry on the cross-disciplinary topic of accountability in software systems. Over two days, attendees engaged in a series of panels, invited talks, and breakout sessions covering: (1) the dimensions of accountability, including legal compliance as well as business and societal aspects and drivers; (2) a conceptual model of the various structures needed to realize accountability; (3) the sources of legal requirements that affect software; (4) the operationalization of legal requirements in software; (5) the requirements to preserve evidence needed to conduct investigations; and (6) a range of challenges and contextual factors beyond software that affect why some accountability structures succeed, while others fail. The workshop was conducted as a collaborative systematization of knowledge that culminated in several research directions. The findings include the importance of clarifying definitions and responsibilities within accountable organizations, which can affect whether those researching accountability are making assumptions that limit the generalizability of findings. Further research was also identified as needed to study the ways to improve the translation of accountability structures into the software design process while improving engagement with stakeholders, such as legislators, regulators, business executives and system developers. Finally, a key finding was the high demands that DASS-like research projects place on interdisciplinary teams: both in terms of team formation and sustainment, as well as, the specific demands of cross-disciplinary learning that covers both research methods, research dissemination, and career development.

</details>


### [14] [Unpredictable Safety: Domain-Dependent Compliance and the Transparency Gap in Open-Weight LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04035v1)
*Zacharie Bugaud*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM安全行为高度依赖领域和框架，合规率跨度大且不可预测，技术框架可绕过安全训练，封闭模型复制结果类似，表明当前安全机制缺乏透明性和一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可信赖的部署需要可预测的安全行为，但现有研究缺乏对开放权重LLM中领域依赖安全行为的系统性理解。

Method: 7个道德领域、7项标准化实验，测试5个开放权重模型（12B-70B），共4,200次交互，采用双条件（分析性框架与操作性框架）和双评判验证；并在GitHub Copilot CLI上对5个封闭模型进行复制实验（n=4,163）。

Result: 合规率从14.7%（人口贩卖）到85.7%（监控设计），跨度71个百分点；同一模型在监控设计上100%合规，在贩卖上仅26.7%；领域内异质性达84.4pp；封闭模型复制显示相同的领域分层但绝对水平更低。

Conclusion: 当前安全机制缺乏透明性和一致性，无法支持可信赖的AI部署。

中文摘要：我们提出了一项关于开放权重大语言模型中领域依赖的安全行为的系统性研究：在7个道德领域中进行7项标准化实验，测试了5个模型（12B–70B），共4,200次交互，并采用双评判验证。使用双条件方法，每个场景分别在分析性框架（识别危害）和操作性框架（帮助实施危害）下进行测试，我们发现合规率从14.7%（人口贩卖）到85.7%（监控设计）不等，跨度达71个百分点，且聚类自助法95%置信区间不重叠。可信赖的部署需要可预测的安全行为，但我们发现合规性高度依赖上下文：同一模型（Mistral Nemo 12B）在100%的请求中提供监控设计，但在协助贩卖方面仅为26.7%。这种不可预测性对部署者来说是不透明的：技术框架绕过，即有害请求被重新表述为工程问题，从而覆盖了安全训练，且没有任何外部信号表明拒绝阈值已发生偏移。领域内异质性高达84.4个百分点，意味着即使在领域层面也无法预测安全行为。对五个前沿封闭模型（GPT-4.1/5.2、Claude Haiku/Sonnet/Opus 4.x；共4,163个响应）的复制实验，通过GitHub Copilot CLI部署产品表面访问，再现了相同的领域分层，绝对水平有所减弱但形状相同，两个低规范化领域（科学欺诈、监控）再次最为宽松。这些结果表明，当前的安全机制缺乏可信赖AI部署所需的透明性和一致性。

Original abstract: We present a systematic study of domain-dependent safety behavior in open-weight LLMs: 7 standardized experiments across 7 ethical domains, testing 5 models (12B--70B) in 4,200 interactions with dual-judge validation. Using a dual-condition methodology, each scenario tested in both an analytical framing (identify the harm) and an operational framing (help commit the harm), we find compliance rates vary from 14.7% (human trafficking) to 85.7% (surveillance design), a 71-percentage-point span with non-overlapping cluster-bootstrapped 95% CIs. Trustworthy deployment requires predictable safety behavior, yet we find compliance is highly context-dependent: the same model (Mistral Nemo 12B) provides surveillance designs in 100% of requests but assists with trafficking in only 26.7%. This unpredictability is opaque to deployers: the technical framing bypass, where harmful requests reframed as engineering problems override safety training without any external signal that refusal thresholds have shifted. Within-domain heterogeneity reaches 84.4pp, meaning safety behavior cannot be predicted even at the domain level. A replication on five frontier closed models (GPT-4.1/5.2, Claude Haiku/Sonnet/Opus 4.x; n=4,163 responses) accessed via the GitHub Copilot CLI deployed-product surface reproduces the same domain stratification, attenuated in absolute level but identical in shape, with the two low-codification domains (science fraud, surveillance) again the most permissive. These results show that current safety mechanisms lack the transparency and consistency required for trustworthy AI deployment.

</details>


### [15] [Many a Little Makes a Mickle: A Code-Centric Empirical Study of Data Minimization Principle in Android App Development](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02960v1)
*Dianshu Liao,Shidong Pan,Zhenchang Xing,Xiaoyu Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过对安卓应用的大规模分析，提炼出31条编码指南以支持数据最小化，并发现LLM生成的代码存在风险，但指南可消除问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺乏在代码层面指导开发者实现隐私原则（尤其是数据最小化）的可操作建议，且现有工作主要关注政策分析。

Method: 对1,114个开源应用进行形成性研究，识别数据最小化场景；对9,875个真实APK进行大规模分析，提炼编码指南；评估LLM代码生成并测试指南效果。

Result: 提炼出31条编码指南；LLM模型复现风险做法，但指南可消除问题。

Conclusion: 倡导在代码级根本原因上响应隐私要求，提升人类和AI辅助编程的合规性。

中文摘要：现代移动应用消耗大量数据以运行，引发了严重的隐私问题和监管挑战。尽管以往的工作主要通过政策分析来检测合规缺口，但缺乏可在代码层面指导开发者实现隐私原则的可操作建议。在本文中，我们聚焦于数据最小化这一可开发者操作的原则，并研究其在安卓应用中的实现。我们对1,114个开源安卓应用进行了形成性研究，识别了五个数据处理阶段中的十个重复出现的数据最小化场景。在此基础上，我们对9,875个真实世界APK进行了大规模分析，提炼出31条可操作的编码指南以支持隐私合规开发。我们进一步研究了基于LLM的安卓开发代码生成，发现最先进的模型持续复现存在数据最小化风险的做法，表明它们继承并放大了真实世界代码中的模式。令人鼓舞的是，纳入我们的指南后，所有评估模型均消除了这些问题。我们的工作倡导转向在代码级根本原因上响应隐私监管要求，从而在人类和AI辅助编程中实现更好的合规性。

Original abstract: Modern mobile applications consume large amounts of data to function, raising significant privacy concerns and regulatory challenges. While prior work has primarily focused on detecting compliance gaps through policy analysis, there remains a lack of actionable guidance for developers to implement privacy principles at the code level. In this paper, we focus on data minimization as a developer-operationalizable principle and investigate its realization in Android applications. We conduct a formative study on 1,114 open-source Android apps to identify ten recurring data minimization scenarios across five data-handling stages. Building on this, we perform a large-scale analysis of 9,875 real-world APKs and distill 31 actionable coding guidelines to support privacy-compliant development. We further examine LLM-based code generation in Android development and find that state-of-the-art models consistently reproduce data minimization-risky practices, indicating that they inherit and amplify patterns from real-world code. Encouragingly, incorporating our guidelines eliminates these issues across all evaluated models. Our work advocates a shift toward responding to privacy regulatory requirements at their code-level root causes, enabling better compliance in both human and AI-assisted programming.

</details>

### [16] [Joint Agent Memory and Exploration Learning via Novelty Signals](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01528v1)
*Shizuo Tian,Xiaohong Weng,Rui Kong,Yuxuan Chen,Guohong Liu,Yuebing Song,Jiacheng Liu,Yuchen Li,Dawei Yin,Ting Cao,Yunxin Liu,Yuanchun Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 联合训练agent记忆与探索，利用新颖性信号，直接提升agent探索能力。

TL;DR: 提出JAMEL框架，通过新颖性驱动的交互联合训练智能体记忆和探索策略，在GUI环境中利用代码覆盖率作为确定性新颖性信号，实现高效探索并减少令牌消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语言模型智能体在开放环境中探索困难，有效的探索需要记忆，但保留原始交互历史计算成本高；潜在记忆可压缩历史，但训练缺乏可靠监督信号。

Method: 通过JAMEL框架联合训练记忆和探索策略，利用新颖性驱动的交互，采用GUI领域中的代码覆盖率作为确定性和持久的新颖性信号，提供无注释的监督。

Result: JAMEL成功泛化到未见环境，探索能力优于开放权重基线，与闭源模型深度相媲美，同时减少令牌消耗。

Conclusion: JAMEL有效结合记忆与探索的相互依赖关系，利用新颖性信号实现无监督的联合学习，提升了探索效率和泛化能力。

中文摘要：在开放环境中，探索是自主智能体的基本能力，但当前的语言模型智能体在此方面存在困难。有效的探索需要记忆，但保留原始交互历史在长轨迹上计算成本高昂。虽然潜在记忆提供了压缩交互历史的解决方案，但其训练缺乏可靠的监督信号。我们提出了联合智能体记忆与探索学习（JAMEL），一个通过新颖性驱动的交互来共同训练智能体记忆和探索策略的框架。我们观察到记忆和探索形成一个相互依赖的循环：持续的探索需要记忆来区分已耗尽的行为和未见过的新行为，而追求新颖性的交互为记忆提供监督，使其对未来探索有用。通过利用确定性和持久的新颖性信号，例如GUI领域中的代码覆盖率，我们为记忆模块提供了自然的、无注释的监督。实证评估表明，JAMEL成功泛化到未见过的环境。其探索能力优于开放权重的基线，并与闭源模型的探索深度相媲美，同时减少了令牌消耗。我们的代码和模型已开源在 https://github.com/MobileLLM/JAMEL。

Original abstract: In open-ended environments, exploration is fundamental for autonomous agents, yet current language model agents struggle with this. Effective exploration requires memory, but retaining raw interaction histories is computationally expensive over long trajectories. While latent memory offers a solution to compress interaction histories, its training lacks reliable supervisory signals. We introduce \textbf{J}oint \textbf{A}gent \textbf{M}emory and \textbf{E}xploration \textbf{L}earning (\textbf{JAMEL}), a framework that trains agentic memory and exploration policy together through novelty-driven interaction. We observe that memory and exploration form a mutually dependent loop: sustained exploration requires memory to distinguish exhausted behaviors from unseen ones, while novelty-seeking interaction provides the supervision needed to make memory useful for future exploration. By utilizing deterministic and persistent novelty signals such as code coverage in the GUI domain, we provide natural, annotation-free supervision for the memory module. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that \ours successfully generalizes to unseen environments. Its exploration capability outperforms open-weight baselines and rivals the exploration depth of a closed-source model while reducing token consumption. Our code and model are open-sourced at https://github.com/MobileLLM/JAMEL.

</details>


### [17] [RoleCDE:Benchmarking and Mitigating Role-Alignment Trade-offs in Role-Playing Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01552v1)
*Huayi Lai,Shichao Song,Simin Niu,Hanyu Wang,Jiawei Yang,Zhouxing Wang,Zhiqiang Yin,Xun Liang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 角色扮演agent基准与微调方法，涉及agent评测和价值对齐。

TL;DR: RoleCDE是一个新基准，用于评估角色扮演代理在角色价值与对齐约束冲突时的决策能力，发现“角色价值解耦”现象，并通过微调缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要评估表面角色保真度，忽视角色对齐价值冲突下的决策能力，因此需要专门基准来填补这一空白。

Method: 构建RoleCDE基准，包含约8000角色和24000困境实例，覆盖三个难度级别和八个角色类别，通过认知困境场景评估角色-场景基础、价值冲突解决和决策倾向。

Result: 主流LLM表现出“角色价值解耦”现象，即默认选择对齐和道德一致决策而非角色特定值；该现象对难度不敏感但因角色类别而异；RoleCDE微调可缓解解耦。

Conclusion: RoleCDE有效评估并揭示角色价值冲突问题，微调可改善价值权衡推理，同时保持角色扮演保真度和通用推理能力。

中文摘要：角色扮演代理（RPA）被广泛用于引导大型语言模型（LLM）表现出角色一致的行为，然而现有的基准测试主要评估表面层面的保真度，对于角色对齐价值冲突下的决策提供有限的洞察。为了弥补这一空白，我们引入了RoleCDE，这是第一个旨在评估RPA在角色特定值与对齐约束之间的结构化冲突下表现的基准测试。RoleCDE将角色感知决策制定形式化为认知困境场景，联合评估角色-场景基础、价值冲突解决和决策倾向。该基准测试大规模构建，覆盖约8000个多样化的角色档案和场景，以及近24000个困境实例，横跨三个难度级别和八个角色类别。对几种主流LLM的评估揭示了一种“角色价值解耦”现象，即当角色特定值与对齐和道德一致性决策发生冲突时，即使有明确的角色条件，代理系统性地默认选择后者。这种行为在很大程度上不受困境难度的影响，但在不同角色类别之间存在显著差异。我们进一步表明，基于RoleCDE的微调通过改进价值权衡推理有效缓解了这种解耦，同时保持了通用的角色扮演保真度和一般推理性能。代码可在 https://github.com/rabbitrose/RoleCDE 获取。

Original abstract: Role-playing agents(RPAs) are widely used to steer large language models(LLMs) toward role-consistent behavior, yet existing benchmarks mainly evaluate surface-level fidelity and offer limited insight into decision making under role-alignment value conflicts. To address this gap, we introduce RoleCDE, the first benchmark designed to evaluate RPAs under structured conflicts between role-specific values and alignment-oriented constraints. RoleCDE formulates role-aware decision making as cognitive dilemma scenarios, jointly evaluating role-scenario grounding, value conflict resolution, and decision tendencies. The benchmark is constructed at scale, covering approximately 8k diverse role profiles and scenarios and nearly 24k dilemma instances across three difficulty levels and eight role categories. Evaluation of several mainstream LLMs reveals a "Role Value Decoupling" phenomenon, where agents systematically default to alignment-and morality-consistent decisions rather than role-specific values when the two conflict, even under explicit role conditioning. This behavior is largely invariant to dilemma difficulty but varies substantially across role categories. We further show that RoleCDE-based fine-tuning effectively mitigates this decoupling by improving value trade-off reasoning, while preserving general role-playing fidelity and general reasoning performance. Code is available at: https://github.com/rabbitrose/RoleCDE.

### [18] [TRON: Targeted Rule-Verifiable Online Environments for Visual Reasoning RL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01599v1)
*Tianze Yang,Yucheng Shi,Ruitong Sun,Jingyuan Huang,Ninghao Liu,Jin Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 为视觉推理RL提供可验证在线环境，可迁移至agent的RL训练。

TL;DR: 提出了TRON在线环境基座，通过可扩展、可验证和可控的训练信号支持视觉推理的强化学习后训练，显著提升了多模态模型的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉RL后训练依赖静态、有限的数据集，缺乏可扩展性、可验证性和可控性，无法按需生成训练实例以适应课程学习。

Method: 设计了TRON基座，包含可控的生成器-验证器程序，按需生成潜在视觉状态、图像、问题和答案，支持无限实例流和课程难度调节；包含520个环境，分为五个能力桶。

Result: 在Qwen3-VL-4B、Qwen2.5-VL-7B和MiMo-VL-7B-SFT上，使用METHOD进行RL后训练在十个外部多模态推理基准上持续提升性能。

Conclusion: TRON为视觉RL后训练提供了可扩展、可验证且可控的在线环境，有效提升了多模态模型在广泛推理任务上的表现。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）用于视觉推理需要可扩展、可验证且可控的训练信号。现有的视觉RL后训练是在静态精心策划的数据集上进行的，这些数据集包含固定的图像-问题-答案样本，受限于其收集预算。在这项工作中，我们引入了TRON（定向、规则可验证的在线环境），一个在线环境基座：一次训练轨迹由可控的生成器-验证器程序按需生成，该程序采样一个新的潜在视觉状态，渲染一张图像，提出一个问题，并精确验证答案。因此，单次运行可以在当前课程所需的难度级别上抽取无限的实例流。当前的TRON套件包含520个环境，组织成五个能力桶（空间、数学、图表、模式/逻辑和计数）；同一基座支持在所有桶上训练的单个完整模型以及每个桶的能力专家模型，无需额外数据收集。我们还引入了基座分析，涵盖生成可靠性、实例和级别多样性、跨环境近乎重复以及基座模型按难度级别的通过率。使用METHOD进行RL后训练在十个外部多模态推理基准上持续提升Qwen3-VL-4B、Qwen2.5-VL-7B和MiMo-VL-7B-SFT的性能。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for visual reasoning needs scalable, verifiable, and controllable training signals. Existing visual RL post-training trains on static curated datasets, with fixed image-question-answer samples bounded by their collection budget. In this work, we introduce TRON (Targeted, Rule-verifiable Online eNvironments), an online environment substrate: a training rollout is generated on demand by a controllable generator-verifier program that samples a fresh latent visual state, renders an image, asks a question, and exactly verifies the answer. A single run can therefore draw an unbounded stream of fresh instances at the difficulty level required by the current curriculum. The current TRON suite contains 520 environments organized into five ability buckets (spatial, mathematical, diagram, pattern/logic, and counting); the same substrate supports both a single full model trained on all buckets and per-bucket ability-specialist models, with no additional data collection. We also introduce a substrate analysis covering generation reliability, instance and level diversity, cross-environment near-duplicates, and base-model pass rate by difficulty level. RL post-training with METHOD consistently improves performance on ten external multimodal reasoning benchmarks across Qwen3-VL-4B, Qwen2.5-VL-7B, and MiMo-VL-7B-SFT.

### [19] [ReSkill: Reconciling Skill Creation with Policy Optimization in Agentic RL](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01619v2)
*Zelin He,Haotian Lin,Boran Han,Wei Zhu,Haoyang Fang,Bernie Wang,Xuan Zhu,Runze Li,Matthew Reimherr*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: agentic RL中技能创建与策略优化，通用方法可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: ReSkill通过将技能创建与策略优化耦合，利用GRPO机制实现技能与策略的协同演化，在多种任务上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能增强RL方法将技能创建与策略优化分离，导致技能可能阻碍而非促进策略学习，需要一种在RL循环内动态调整技能的方法。

Method: 提出ReSkill框架，基于GRPO的组内结构，包含三个机制：断言驱动的技能创建器、组内轨迹采样、以及自适应折扣的Thompson采样，实现技能与策略的联合优化。

Result: 在多领域实验中，ReSkill持续优于现有记忆和技能基RL方法，尤其在未见任务上表现突出；技能生命周期分析验证了技能自动创建、测试、精炼和修剪的协同演化过程。

Conclusion: ReSkill实现了技能与策略的协同演化，证明了在强化学习过程中动态调整技能的有效性，为LLM代理积累可重用策略提供了新范式。

中文摘要：智能体强化学习（RL）使LLM代理能够从环境奖励中持续改进，但所得到的策略并未系统地积累跨任务泛化的可重用策略。模块化技能可以提供此类可重用策略，然而现有的技能增强RL方法将技能创建与策略优化解耦，导致可能采用与不断演化的策略相冲突的技能。受Anthropic的Skill Creator启发，我们提出了ReSkill，一种RL循环中的技能创建框架，协调技能演化与策略学习。ReSkill利用GRPO的组内结构，仅以边际额外开销自然地嵌入三种机制：（1）断言驱动的技能创建器，从过去经验中诊断失败并提出条件性的、基于触发器的技能修订；（2）组内轨迹采样，实现对技能版本的可控比较，捕捉哪个版本最能支持策略的持续学习；以及（3）具有自适应折扣的Thompson采样，在策略演化过程中平衡技能版本选择的探索与利用。在多个领域中，ReSkill持续优于现有的基于记忆和技能的RL方法，在未见任务上取得最大提升。对技能生命周期的分析表明，随着策略改进，技能会被自动创建、测试、改进和修剪，展示了协调的技能-策略协同演化。

Original abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning (RL) enables LLM agents to improve continuously from environment rewards, yet the resulting policies do not systematically accumulate reusable strategies that generalize across tasks. Modular skills can provide such reusable strategies, yet existing skill-augmented RL methods decouple skill creation from policy optimization, risking adopting skills that conflict with the evolving policy. Inspired by Anthropic's Skill Creator, we introduce ReSkill, an RL-in-the-loop skill creation framework that reconciles skill evolution with policy learning. ReSkill exploits the group-wise structure of GRPO to naturally embed three mechanisms with only marginal additional overhead: (1) an assertion-driven skill creator that diagnoses failures from past experience and proposes conditional, trigger-based skill revisions; (2) within-group rollout sampling that enables controlled comparison of skill versions, capturing which version best supports the policy's ongoing learning; and (3) Thompson Sampling with adaptive discounting to balance exploration and exploitation in skill version selection as the policy evolves. Across several domains, ReSkill consistently outperforms existing memory and skill-based RL methods, with the largest gains on unseen tasks. Analysis of the skill lifecycle shows skills being automatically created, tested, refined, and pruned as the policy improves, demonstrating reconciled skill-policy co-evolution.

### [20] [MobEvolve: An Agentic Self-Evolving Heuristic System for Interpretable Human Mobility Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01640v1)

Original abstract: Human mobility generation aims to synthesize realistic trip chains for target populations based on individual features. To bridge this gap, we introduce MobEvolve, the first agentic self-evolving heuristic framework for human mobility generation. MobEvolve initializes a behavior-inspired heuristic system and employs an LLM agent to iteratively evolve its internal logic. By diagnosing empirical misalignments and failure cases on a validation set, the agent proposes targeted updates and accumulates evolution memory for cumulative self-improvement. Extensive evaluations on the Singapore and Montreal benchmarks demonstrate that MobEvolve significantly outperforms state-of-the-art deep generative and LLM-based methods in individual trajectory fidelity, population-level distribution alignment, and behavioral plausibility, while preserving interpretability and high inference efficiency.

*Donghwan Kim,Prakhar Singh,Younghoon Min,Jongryool Kim,Jongse Park,Kiwan Maeng*

Original abstract: Agentic AI completes tasks through iterative planning, tool use, and reasoning based on observed outcomes. Despite its popularity, its system-level behavior remains poorly understood, particularly for complex datasets and agent architectures-owing to highly non-deterministic execution, prohibitive evaluation costs, and limited visibility into proprietary models. This paper presents GAIATrace, the first token-level trace dataset of two state-of-the-art agentic systems (MiroThinker and OWL) running GAIA, a benchmark composed of a heterogeneous mix of general-purpose tasks. Unlike prior trace datasets, GAIATrace captures full reasoning tokens, task-level structures, and activities of every major participating LLMs, enabling in-depth systems research. Complementing the dataset, we present Vidur-Agent, a trace-driven simulator that can replay GAIATrace to perform reproducible, low-cost system evaluation across diverse simulated environments. Using both artifacts, we characterize how modern agentic systems handle general tasks and how various system design choices shape their behavior, yielding several unique findings.

### [22] [TriAlign: Towards Universal Truth Consistency in Personalized LLM Alignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01755v1)
*Thi-Nhung Nguyen,Linhao Luo,Rollin Omari,Junae Kim,Thuy-Trang Vu,Dinh Phung*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多智能体强化学习框架用于对齐，可迁移至coding agent协作。

TL;DR: 提出TriAlign框架，通过离线多智能体强化学习在个性化大语言模型中实现普遍真值的跨群体一致性与个性化之间的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有个性化大语言模型在适应不同用户时，会导致客观任务上不同社交群体之间普遍真值的不一致性，而现有对齐方法忽视了这一公平性问题。

Method: 提出TriAlign，一个离线多智能体强化学习框架，将每个社交群体建模为智能体，通过公平性感知目标和显式不一致性惩罚共同优化真值准确性、跨群体一致性和个性化。

Result: 在多个基准上，TriAlign相比强基线在三个目标之间取得更优平衡，降低了跨群体的真值差异，同时提升了客观任务性能和个性化质量。

Conclusion: TriAlign有效解决了个性化LLM中普遍真值的公平性问题，为个性化与一致性平衡提供了可行方案。

中文摘要：个性化大语言模型根据用户的偏好和社会属性调整响应，但可能在社交群体之间引入显著的普遍真值不一致性，其中某些群体在客观任务上系统性地获得较不准确的响应。现有的对齐方法要么忽略个性化，要么主要关注主观偏好对齐，在很大程度上忽视了普遍真值中的公平性和一致性。为了解决这一差距，我们研究了真值不变对齐（TIA），这是一个针对个性化LLM的对齐问题，旨在确保普遍真值在不同社交群体之间保持一致，同时保持个性化。我们提出了TriAlign，这是第一个用于TIA的离线多智能体强化学习（MARL）框架，其中每个社交群体被建模为一个交互的智能体。TriAlign通过一个公平性感知目标和一个显式的不一致性惩罚，共同优化普遍真值准确性、跨群体真值一致性和个性化。跨不同基准的实验表明，TriAlign在这三个目标之间实现了比强基线更强的平衡，减少了跨社交群体的普遍真值差异，同时提高了客观任务性能和个性化质量。

Original abstract: Personalized large language models adapt responses to users' preferences and social attributes, but can introduce substantial universal truth inconsistencies across social groups, where some groups systematically receive less accurate responses on objective tasks. Existing alignment methods either ignore personalization or mainly focus on subjective preference alignment, largely overlooking fairness and consistency in universal truths. To address this gap, we study Truth-Invariant Alignment (TIA), an alignment problem for personalized LLMs that aims to ensure universal truths remain consistent across social groups while preserving personalization. We propose TriAlign, the first offline multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) framework for TIA, where each social group is modeled as an agent interacting. TriAlign jointly optimizes universal truth accuracy, cross-group truth consistency, and personalization through a fairness-aware objective and an explicit inconsistency penalty. Experiments across diverse benchmarks demonstrate that TriAlign achieves a stronger balance among these three objectives than strong baselines, reducing universal truth disparities across social groups while improving both objective task performance and personalization quality.

### [23] [OctoT2I: A Self-Evolving Agentic Text-to-Image Router](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01803v1)
*Xu Jiang,Bin Chen,Gehui Li,Yule Duan,Ronggang Wang,Jian Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自进化agentic T2I路由框架，包含规划、记忆、自改进机制，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出OctoT2I代理框架，通过自进化机制和多轮路由策略联合优化T2I生成质量与推理效率，在GenEval上达到0.96，推理速度提升90.3%，能效提升56.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有T2I模型面临边际收益递减，代理式方法依赖昂贵先验、决策僵化且忽略效率，急需高效灵活的框架。

Method: 构建OctoT2I框架，包含有状态多轮路由策略和自进化机制（自主定义概念维度+PSEL循环探索工具能力边界）。

Result: 在GenEval上得分0.96，相比Flow-GRPO实现90.3%推理加速和56.6%能效提升。

Conclusion: OctoT2I有效平衡了T2I任务的性能与效率，且无需人工监督，具有实用性和扩展性。

中文摘要：文本到图像（Text-to-Image, T2I）模型的爆炸性增长，从大规模版本到轻量级、实时模型，如今正面临单一模型扩展带来的边际收益递减问题。代理式T2I方法通过使用多个模型来缓解这一瓶颈。然而，现有的代理式T2I方法面临三个关键挑战：依赖昂贵的手工先验或人工标注、僵化的单路径决策机制以及忽略推理效率。为了解决这些挑战，我们引入了OctoT2I，一个新颖的代理框架，将T2I任务重新表述为生成质量和推理效率的联合优化。OctoT2I实现了一种有状态的多轮路由策略，该策略根据其知识和记忆自适应地选择最合适的工具。这一策略由我们新颖的自我进化机制从头构建的知识库所支撑。该机制无需人工监督，首先自主定义基础概念维度（例如风格、颜色、数量），然后通过迭代的“提出-解决-评估-学习”（PSEL）循环智能地探索其组合。PSEL循环高效地发现每个工具的能力边界，推动无需外部指导的持续改进。大量实验表明，OctoT2I在GenEval上达到了具有竞争力的性能（0.96），同时在领先基线（Flow-GRPO）上实现了90.3%的推理速度提升和56.6%的能效增益，达到了性能与效率的出色平衡。代码和模型将公开提供。

Original abstract: The explosive growth of Text-to-Image (T2I) models, from large-scale versions to lightweight, real-time ones, now faces diminishing marginal returns from single-model scaling. Agentic T2I methods emerged to alleviate this bottleneck by using multiple models. However, existing agentic T2I methods suffer from three key challenges: reliance on expensive handcrafted priors or human annotations, rigid single-path decision mechanisms, and a neglect of inference efficiency. To address these challenges, we introduce OctoT2I, a novel agentic framework that reformulates the T2I task as a joint optimization of generation quality and inference efficiency. OctoT2I implements a stateful, multi-round routing strategy that adaptively selects the most suitable tool based on its knowledge and memory. This strategy is enabled by a knowledge base built from scratch by our novel Self-Evolving Mechanism. This mechanism, which requires no human supervision, first autonomously defines foundational Conceptual Dimensions (eg, style, color, count) and then intelligently explores their combinations via an iterative" Propose--Solve--Evaluate--Learn"(PSEL) loop. The PSEL loop efficiently discovers each tool's capability frontier, driving continuous improvement without external guidance. Extensive experiments demonstrate that OctoT2I achieves competitive performance (0.96) on GenEval while delivering a 90.3% inference speedup and a 56.6% energy-efficiency gain over the leading baseline (Flow-GRPO), striking an exceptional balance between performance and efficiency. Code and models will be made available.

</details>


### [24] [Token Predictors Are Not Planners: Building Physically Grounded Causal Reasoners](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01810v1)
*Zheng Lu,Mingqi Gao,Qinlei Xie,Wanqi Zhong,Hanwen Cui,Heng Cao,Zirui Song,Yifan Yang,Chong Luo,Bei Liu,Yiming Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出因果规划基准和训练方法，推动agent从token预测到因果推理，改善agent规划能力。

TL;DR: 提出Causal-Plan-Bench和Causal-Plan-1M，通过因果推理训练使模型Causal Planner在物理规划上显著提升，并发现因果缩放定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身规划基准偏向语言预测而非物理因果推理，导致模型依赖统计先验而缺乏真正物理自主性。

Method: 构建Causal-Plan-Bench（四维因果诊断套件）和Causal-Plan-1M（百万级推理轨迹语料库），采用四阶段标注流水线在自我中心视频上生成数据，并用因果训练配方微调Qwen3-VL-8B得到Causal Planner。

Result: Causal Planner在域内和跨基准任务上表现优异，且训练数据从33.22提升到45.28（相对增益36.3%），揭示了因果缩放定律。

Conclusion: 从基于语言的词符预测转向基于物理的因果推理是实现具身智能体真正物理能动性的关键步骤。

中文摘要：当前具身视觉-语言规划的基准通常有利于基于语言的下一个词符预测，而不是基于物理的下一个状态推理。这奖励了模仿统计语言先验而非跟踪因果依赖的模型，将物理规划降级为浅层序列建模。我们认为，可靠的物理自主性需要从基于语言的词符预测转向基于物理的因果推理。为此，我们引入了Causal-Plan-Bench，这是一个通过多阶段验证策划的高保真诊断套件，用于评估跨四个因果维度的具身规划。我们还构建了Causal-Plan-1M，一个百万规模的显式推理轨迹语料库，通过四阶段标注流水线在自我中心视频上生成。广泛评估表明，领先模型仍然难以展示真正的物理能动性，Gemini 3 Pro在我们的基准上仅达到38.18。相比之下，我们的训练方案使基于Qwen3-VL-8B构建的Causal Planner能够内化物理逻辑，以实现更准确的下一状态估计。该模型实现了强大的域内性能和跨基准泛化，并揭示了因果缩放定律：将因果训练数据扩展到一百万实例带来了36.3%的相对提升，从33.22到45.28。总体而言，我们的工作为将智能体从表面的词符预测器转变为基于物理的因果推理者迈出了具体的一步。

Original abstract: Current benchmarks for embodied vision-language planning often favor linguistic next-token prediction over physically grounded next-state reasoning. This rewards models that mimic statistical language priors rather than track causal dependencies, reducing physical planning to shallow sequence modeling. We argue that reliable physical autonomy requires a shift from linguistically grounded token prediction toward physically grounded causal reasoning. To this end, we introduce Causal-Plan-Bench, a high-fidelity diagnostic suite curated through multi-stage verification to evaluate embodied planning across four causal dimensions. We also construct Causal-Plan-1M, a million-scale corpus of explicit reasoning traces produced by a four-stage annotation pipeline over egocentric videos. Extensive evaluation shows that leading models still struggle to demonstrate genuine physical agency, with Gemini 3 Pro reaching only 38.18 on our benchmark. In contrast, our training recipe enables Causal Planner, built on Qwen3-VL-8B, to internalize physical logic for more accurate next-state estimation. The model achieves strong in-domain performance and cross-benchmark generalization, and reveals a Causal Scaling Law: scaling causal training data to one million instances yields a 36.3% relative gain, from 33.22 to 45.28. Overall, our work provides a concrete step toward turning agents from superficial token predictors into physically grounded causal reasoners.

### [25] [CAPF: Guiding Search-Agent Rollouts with Credit-Attenuated Privileged Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01830v1)
*Bin Chen,Xinye Liao,Yiming Liu,Xin Liao,Chonghan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: CAPF方法通过特权反馈改进搜索agent的RL训练，直接提升agent推理能力。

TL;DR: 提出CAPF机制，利用验证器侧特权反馈改善RLVR训练中的稀疏奖励问题，提升LLM搜索智能体性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在困难问题上，端到端成功轨迹稀少，导致结果奖励稀疏，仅依赖结果奖励的RLVR难以有效学习。

Method: 提出训练时机制CAPF，通过特权反馈调用提供验证器侧信息，将零奖励尝试修正为正奖励修复轨迹，并衰减反馈调用和早期动作的信用以适应部署。

Result: 在七个开放域QA基准上，Qwen3-4B的平均精确匹配分数从44.7%提升至48.5%。

Conclusion: CAPF利用验证器侧信息改善了RLVR在困难问题上的学习，显著提升了搜索增强推理性能。

中文摘要：最近的LLM搜索智能体使用带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）从结果奖励中学习搜索增强推理。在困难问题上，这些智能体很少采样到端到端成功的轨迹，使得仅依赖结果的RLVR只有少量正奖励轨迹。我们认为，在此类问题上改进学习需要在训练期间提供额外指导，而RLVR已经包含可以提供这种指导的验证器侧信息。这些信息可以识别智能体提交答案中的错误或遗漏，并引导轨迹内的修正。我们提出一种名为**信用衰减特权反馈**（CAPF）的训练时机制，该机制通过在训练期间进行特权反馈调用，使验证器侧信息可用。CAPF允许策略将零奖励尝试修正为正奖励修复轨迹，并衰减对反馈调用和早期动作的信用，以适应没有此调用的部署。实证研究表明，在七个开放域问答基准上，CAPF将Qwen3-4B的平均精确匹配分数从仅结果RLVR的44.7%提升至48.5%。

Original abstract: Recent LLM search agents use reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) to learn search-augmented reasoning from outcome rewards. On hard problems, these agents rarely sample end-to-end successful rollouts, leaving outcome-only RLVR with few positive-reward trajectories. We argue that improving learning on such problems requires additional guidance during training, and RLVR already contains verifier-side information that can provide it. This information can identify errors or omissions in the agent's submitted answer and guide revision within the rollout. We propose a training-time mechanism called \textbf{Credit-Attenuated Privileged Feedback} (CAPF), which makes this verifier-side information available through a Privileged Feedback call during training. CAPF lets the policy revise zero-reward attempts into positive-reward repair trajectories and attenuates credit for the feedback call and earlier actions to accommodate deployment without this call. Empirical research demonstrates that CAPF improves Qwen3-4B's average exact-match score from 44.7% under outcome-only RLVR to 48.5% on seven open-domain QA benchmarks.

</details>


### [26] [WorldCoder-Bench: Benchmarking Physically Grounded 3D World Synthesis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01869v2)
*Shuo Lu,Yinuo Xu,Kecheng Yu,Siru Jiang,Yongcan Yu,Yubin Wang,Haitao Yang,Yuxiang Zhang,Bin Wang,Ran He,Jian Liang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估LLM agent生成物理3D世界，涉及代码合成、执行验证，与coding agent相关。

TL;DR: 提出了WorldCoder-Bench基准和StateProbe评估协议，用于测试LLM生成可执行3D世界的能力，发现现有模型在状态模式保持和交互链完整性上表现不佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有web生成基准仅观察像素或DOM，无法评估Three.js动态3D世界的真实行为，需要新的基准和评估方法。

Method: 构建包含2026个任务的WorldCoder-Bench基准，提出基于执行的StateProbe协议，在沙盒浏览器中验证隐藏的运行时契约。

Result: 最佳模型在WorldCoder-Core上验证覆盖率仅27.8%，在Robust版本上19.9%，失败主因是状态模式漂移和交互链断裂。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在生成复杂3D交互世界方面能力有限，但廉价模型在简单领域仍有价值；基准开源供后续研究。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被要求不仅编写静态界面，还要从自然语言构建可执行的交互式世界。浏览器原生3D（通常使用Three.js构建）是下一个自然前沿：生成的程序必须集成资产，遵守空间和物理约束，并保持用户面向的控件与隐藏的运行时状态同步。然而，现有的网络生成基准和评估器大多只观察像素或DOM节点，而Three.js世界的机制则在一个不透明的<canvas>内部展开。我们引入了WorldCoder-Bench，一个用于自主、物理基础的3D世界合成的基准。WorldCoder-Bench包含2,026个专家精心策划的任务，涵盖模拟、渲染和应用场景，并带有可选的.glb资产和隐藏的行为契约。我们进一步提出了StateProbe，一种基于执行的协议，它在沙盒浏览器中探测生成的程序，并验证运行时状态和转换上的隐藏、突变加固的契约。除了验证覆盖率，我们还报告了自动化回报和时间效率乘数，以衡量正确性调整后的成本和时间节省。在九个前沿模型中，最佳系统在WorldCoder-Core上仅达到27.8%的验证覆盖率，在WorldCoder-Robust上达到19.9%，失败主要源于状态模式漂移和断裂的交互链，而非缺失场景元素。效用指标进一步表明，廉价或快速的模型在较简单的领域仍能提供显著价值。WorldCoder-Bench可在https://anonymous.4open.science/r/WorldCoder-Bench/获取。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly asked not only to write static interfaces, but to construct executable interactive worlds from natural language. Browser-native 3D, commonly built with Three.js, is a natural next frontier: generated programs must integrate assets, obey spatial and physical constraints, and keep user-facing controls synchronized with hidden runtime state. Existing web-generation benchmarks and evaluators, however, largely observe only pixels or DOM nodes, while the mechanics of a Three.js world unfold inside an opaque <canvas>. We introduce WorldCoder-Bench, a benchmark for autonomous, physically grounded 3D world synthesis. WorldCoder-Bench contains 2,026 expert-curated tasks across Simulation, Rendering, and Application scenarios, with optional .glb assets and hidden behavioral contracts. We further propose StateProbe, an execution-based protocol that probes generated programs in a sandboxed browser and verifies hidden, mutation-hardened contracts over runtime states and transitions. Beyond verification coverage, we report Return on Automation and Time Efficiency Multiplier to measure correctness-adjusted cost and time savings. Across nine frontier models, the best system reaches only 27.8% verification coverage on WorldCoder-Core and 19.9% on WorldCoder-Robust, with failures dominated by state-schema drift and broken interaction chains rather than missing scene elements. Utility metrics further show that cheap or fast models can still provide substantial value on easier domains. WorldCoder-Bench is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/WorldCoder-Bench/.

</details>


### [27] [Absorbing Complexity: An Interaction-Native Knowledge Harness for Financial LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01886v1)
*Ailiya Borjigin,Igor Stadnyk,Ben Bilski,Maksym Chikita,Dmytro Kyrylenko,Sofiia Pidturkina,Julia Stadnyk*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 金融LLM agent的知识管理框架，涉及记忆、知识注入、审计，可迁移到coding agent设计。

TL;DR: InKH通过被动知识注入、时态图记忆和失效机制，将金融AI代理的复杂管理从用户转移到系统，显著降低延迟、成本和陈旧知识使用，提升任务质量与可追溯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融AI代理让用户承担复杂度，导致上下文遗忘、重复错误和审计困难，亟需将复杂性吸收到系统中的架构。

Method: 提出InKH架构，包含被动知识注入、时态图记忆、维基审计表面和后台提取与失效机制，将事件转化为结构化知识。

Result: 在合成基准上，InKH在900ms延迟下达到0.815任务质量，相较于基线大幅降低延迟、成本和陈旧知识使用，提升质量和可追溯性。

Conclusion: 金融AI的采用关键在于系统吸收复杂度而非转嫁给用户，架构验证了行为有效性，但非实时交易性能。

中文摘要：金融AI代理常常因为一个简单的原因而失败：它们让用户承担复杂性。用户必须反复陈述目标、风险偏好、投资组合背景、过去的判断以及不断变化的市场假设，而代理则回答、检索、行动然后遗忘。在金融领域，这不仅仅是方便性问题。在市场分析、跟单交易审查和交易准备等任务中，遗忘的上下文和陈旧的记忆会导致延迟、重复错误、审计能力弱以及不安全的决策。我们提出了交互原生知识利用系统（InKH），一种用于金融LLM代理的架构，将复杂性吸收到系统中。InKH将用户、市场、投资组合和工具事件转化为结构化的操作知识。它使用被动知识注入在主要模型步骤之前组装限定的工作上下文缓冲区，用于低延迟检索的时态图记忆，用于人类可读治理的维基审计表面，以及具有成熟度、衰减和写入时无效化的后台提取。我们在一个可复现的受控合成基准上评估InKH，该基准具有24个随机种子、4轮、每轮80个episode和6个基线，产生了46,080个基线条件评估。InKH在900毫秒延迟下实现了0.815的平均任务质量。与代理驱动的维基漫步记忆相比，它将延迟降低了82.95%，代币成本降低了82.29%，陈旧知识使用量降低了96.58%，同时质量提高了0.108，可追溯性提高了0.461。与没有失效机制的时态图系统相比，它提高了0.050的质量，并将陈旧记忆使用量降低了96.58%，服务成本相当。结果支持了金融AI的设计论点：当复杂性被系统吸收而不是转移给用户时，采用才会发生。该基准验证了架构层面的行为，而非实时交易性能。

Original abstract: Financial AI agents often fail for a simple reason: they make users carry the complexity. A user must repeatedly restate goals, risk preferences, portfolio context, past judgments, and shifting market assumptions, while the agent answers, retrieves, acts, and forgets. In finance, this is not just inconvenient. In tasks such as market analysis, copy-trading review, and trade preparation, forgotten context and stale memory can create latency, repeated errors, weak auditability, and unsafe decisions.
  We propose the interaction-native knowledge harness (InKH), an architecture for financial LLM agents that absorbs complexity into the system. InKH converts user, market, portfolio, and tool events into structured operational knowledge. It uses passive knowledge injection to assemble a bounded working context buffer before the main model step, temporal graph memory for low-latency retrieval, a wiki audit surface for human-readable governance, and background extraction with maturity, decay, and write-time invalidation.
  We evaluate InKH on a reproducible controlled synthetic benchmark with 24 random seeds, 4 rounds, 80 episodes per round, and 6 baselines, producing 46,080 baseline-conditioned evaluations. InKH achieves mean task quality of 0.815 at 900 ms latency. Compared with agent-driven wiki-walk memory, it reduces latency by 82.95 percent, token cost by 82.29 percent, and stale-knowledge usage by 96.58 percent, while improving quality by 0.108 and traceability by 0.461. Compared with a temporal-graph system without invalidation, it improves quality by 0.050 and reduces stale-memory usage by 96.58 percent with comparable serving cost.
  The results support a design thesis for financial AI: adoption happens when complexity is absorbed by the system rather than transferred to the user. The benchmark validates architecture-level behavior, not live trading performance.

</details>


### [28] [SMH-Bench: Benchmarking LLM Agents for Environment-Grounded Reasoning and Action in Smart Homes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01912v1)
*Kuan Li,Shuo Zhang,Huacan Wang,Fangzhou Yu,Zecheng Sheng,Yi Gu,Weipeng Ming,Lei Xue,Chen Liu,Sen Hu,Ronghao Chen,Siyue Lin,Yuqing Hou,Xiaofeng Mou,Yi Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 智能家居LLM agent benchmark，规划与推理，可直接迁移至coding agent评测。

TL;DR: 提出了SMH-Bench，一个基于可执行模拟器的智能家居LLM评估基准，包含1100个任务，发现前沿LLMs在显式任务上表现良好但在复杂推理上存在弱点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能家居基准无法评估LLMs在现实家庭场景中的推理、交互和可靠行动能力，局限于静态指令映射或有限模拟。

Method: 构建了可执行且可验证的智能家居模拟器HomeEnv，并设计了包含1100个任务、7个类别和22个子类别的SMH-Bench基准，任务按家庭复杂度分层。

Result: 前沿LLMs在显式控制和查询任务上表现强劲，但在自动化任务调度、歧义处理和个人化推理上显著较弱，且随着家庭复杂度增加性能下降。

Conclusion: SMH-Bench有望促进更可靠、上下文感知且实际可部署的智能家居代理的发展。

中文摘要：智能家居正朝着复杂的状态依赖生活环境发展，需要大型语言模型（LLMs）推理用户意图、偏好和多设备交互。然而，现有的智能家居基准测试通常聚焦于静态指令到API的映射或有限模拟，未能评估LLMs在现实家庭场景中推理、交互和可靠行动的能力。为解决这些限制，我们引入SMH-Bench，一个用于评估LLMs在智能家居环境中综合能力的基准。基于可执行且可验证的智能家居模拟器HomeEnv，SMH-Bench包含1100个高质量任务，涵盖7个类别和22个细粒度子类别。它进一步将任务分层为简单、中等和复杂家庭，从小型公寓到拥有135个设备的密集多房间环境。实验表明，尽管前沿LLMs在显式控制和查询任务上表现强劲，但在自动化任务调度、歧义处理和个人化推理方面仍存在显著弱点，尤其是随着家庭复杂性的增加。我们希望SMH-Bench将促进更可靠、上下文感知且实际可部署的智能家居代理的发展。

Original abstract: Smart homes are evolving toward complex state-dependent living environments, requiring Large Language Models (LLMs) to reason over user intent, preferences, and multi-device interactions. However, existing smart-home benchmarks often focus on static instruction-to-API mapping or limited simulations, failing to evaluate whether LLMs can reason, interact, and act reliably in realistic household scenarios. To address these limitations, we introduce SMH-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark for evaluating LLMs in smart-home environments. Built upon HomeEnv, an executable and verifiable smart-home simulator, SMH-Bench contains 1,100 high-quality tasks spanning 7 categories and 22 fine-grained subcategories. It further stratifies tasks across simple, medium and complex homes, ranging from small apartments to dense multi-room environments with 135 devices. Experiments show that although frontier LLMs achieve strong performance on explicit control and query tasks, they still exhibit significant weaknesses in automation task scheduling, ambiguity handling and personalized reasoning, especially as home complexity increases. We hope SMH-Bench will facilitate the development of more reliable, context-aware, and practically deployable smart-home agents.

### [29] [AutoMedBench: Towards Medical AutoResearch with Agentic AI Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01961v2)
*Junqi Liu,Selena Song,Yuhan Wang,Jiawei Mao,Hardy Chen,Xiaoke Huang,Tianhao Qi,Pengfei Guo,Yucheng Tang,Yufan He,Can Zhao,Andriy Myronenko,Dong Yang,Daguang Xu,Yuyin Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 医学自主研究benchmark (AutoMedBench)，包含多阶段agent工作流，可迁移至软件工程agent评估。

TL;DR: 提出AutoMedBench，一个工作流程感知的基准，通过五阶段评分揭示医学AI智能体在验证环节最弱，而设置环节最强，且验证和提交错误主导失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 验证阶段平均得分最低，设置阶段最高；验证和提交错误分别占37.7%和38.1%，任务理解错误仅0.9%；有错误代码的运行平均得分低48%。

Conclusion: 当前智能体更擅长执行流程而非验证可靠性，验证和提交是主要瓶颈。

中文摘要：自主智能体越来越被期望支持端到端的医学AI研究工作流程，而不仅仅是孤立的预测任务或短格式的临床问题回答。然而，现有的医学智能体基准主要评估最终输出，对智能体在研究过程中的行为可见性有限。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了AutoMedBench，一个面向自主医学AI研究的工作流程感知基准，涵盖多种医学成像和多模态推理任务，将智能体执行组织成一个统一的五阶段工作流程（S1-S5）：计划、设置、验证、推理和提交。它包含长时程任务，每次运行平均33个智能体轮次，跨越五个研究方向：分割、图像增强、视觉问答（VQA）、报告生成和病变检测。每个任务在两个难度级别（Lite和Standard）下评估，使用相同的数据和指标，但任务简报的脚手架数量不同，每次运行使用最终任务性能和S1-S5阶段得分进行评分，从而实现对从初始任务简报到最终提交工件的阶段级分析。在数千次记录运行中，阶段级得分显示验证（Validate）是平均而言最弱的工作流程阶段，而设置（Setup）是最强的，这表明当前智能体更擅长使流程可执行，而不是验证其可靠性。运行后的错误分析进一步表明，验证和提交失败主导了标记的错误，分别占触发代码的37.7%和38.1%，而任务理解错误罕见，仅占0.9%，且有一次触发错误代码的运行平均得分比无错误代码的运行低48%。

Original abstract: Autonomous agents are increasingly expected to support end-to-end medical-AI research workflows, moving beyond isolated prediction tasks or short-form clinical question answering. However, existing medical agent benchmarks primarily evaluate final outputs, providing limited visibility into agent behavior within the research process. To address this gap, we present AutoMedBench, a workflow-aware benchmark for autonomous medical-AI research across diverse medical imaging and multimodal inference tasks, organizing agent execution into a unified five-stage workflow (S1-S5): Plan, Setup, Validate, Inference, and Submit. It comprises long-horizon tasks with each run averaging 33 agent turns, spanning five research tracks: segmentation, image enhancement, visual question answering (VQA), report generation, and lesion detection. Each task is evaluated under two difficulty tiers, Lite and Standard, which use the same data and metrics but differ in the amount of task-brief scaffolding, and each run is scored using both final task performance and S1-S5 stage scores, enabling stage-level analysis from the initial task brief to the final submitted artifact. Across thousands of recorded runs, stage-level scoring reveals that Validate is the weakest workflow stage on average, whereas Setup is the strongest, suggesting that current agents are better at making pipelines executable than at verifying their reliability. Post-run error analysis further shows that verification and submission failures dominate tagged errors, accounting for 37.7% and 38.1% of fired codes respectively, whereas task-understanding errors are rare at 0.9%, and runs with one fired error code have a 48% lower overall score than runs with no error code on average.

### [31] [SafeMCP: Proactive Power Regulation for LLM Agent Defense via Environment-Grounded Look-Ahead Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01991v1)
*Lichao Wang,Zhaoxing Ren,Tianzhuo Yang,Jiaming Ji,Chi Harold Liu,Yaodong Yang,Juntao Dai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出SafeMCP防御框架，利用前瞻推理约束LLM agent工具使用，可迁移至agent安全控制。

TL;DR: SafeMCP是一种服务器端防御插件，通过前瞻推理和两层防御机制（主动过滤和即时干预）约束LLM代理工具获取，并采用三阶段训练（环境动态基础、安全策略初始化、双重奖励强化学习）以平衡安全与效用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理在MCP协议下行动空间扩展导致权力寻求风险，微小错误可能引发灾难性故障，现有方法缺乏对工具获取的预测性安全约束。

Method: SafeMCP使用内部世界模型进行前瞻推理，实现主动工具过滤和即时干预两层防御；训练采用三阶段：环境动态基础、安全策略初始化和双重可验证奖励的强化学习。

Result: 在PowerSeeking Bench、ToolEmu和AgentHarm基准上，SafeMCP在有效缓解风险的同时保持了代理的效用，实现了安全平衡。

Conclusion: SafeMCP成功地在LLM代理的广阔行动空间与安全约束之间取得平衡，验证了预测性工具过滤和即时干预的有效性。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）代理越来越多地利用模型上下文协议（MCP）在复杂环境中运行，其行动空间的扩展为代理提供了不安全的操作能力，并凸显了权力寻求的风险。虽然广阔的行动空间和更大的环境影响对于任务完成至关重要，但它们创造了一个脆弱的风险面，其中微小的错误或幻觉会被放大为灾难性故障。为此，我们提出了SafeMCP，一种服务器端防御插件，通过预测性推理关于未来安全风险来约束工具获取。SafeMCP利用内部世界模型进行前瞻推理，实现两层防御：主动工具过滤以约束危险权力扩展，以及即时干预作为故障安全机制。为了训练SafeMCP，我们引入了一个三阶段流程，包括环境动态基础、安全策略初始化和具有双重可验证奖励的强化学习（RL）。在PowerSeeking Bench、ToolEmu和AgentHarm上的实验表明，SafeMCP实现了安全平衡，有效缓解风险同时保持代理效用。

Original abstract: As Large Language Model (LLM) agents increasingly leverage the Model Context Protocol (MCP) to operate in complex environments, the expansion of their action spaces offers agents unsafe capabilities and underscores the risk of power-seeking. While broad action space and greater environment influence are essential for task fulfillment, they create a fragile risk surface where minor errors or hallucinations are magnified into catastrophic failures. In response, we propose SafeMCP, a {server-side} defense plugin that constrains tool acquisition via predictive reasoning regarding future safety risks. SafeMCP utilizes an internal world model for look-ahead reasoning to implement a two-tier defense: proactive tool filtering to constrain hazardous power expansion and immediate intervention as a fail-safe. To train SafeMCP, we introduce a three-stage pipeline comprising environmental dynamic grounding, safe policy initialization, and reinforcement learning (RL) with dual verifiable rewards. Experiments on PowerSeeking Bench, ToolEmu, and AgentHarm show that SafeMCP achieves a safe equilibrium, effectively mitigating risks while preserving agent utility.
