### [64] [Handoff Debt: The Rediscovery Cost When Coding Agents Take Over Interrupted Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02875v1)
*Dipesh KC,Anjila Budathoki*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究coding agent任务中断接手成本，直接相关于代码agent评估

TL;DR: 引入“交接债务”概念和接管协议，实验表明上下文交接显著降低代理恢复成本，但解决率变化不大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编码代理基准忽略了实际工作中的任务中断和恢复成本，需要量化前任工作不透明带来的额外代价。

Method: 设计接管协议，在确定性交接点中断代理，提供四种交接视图（仅仓库状态、原始轨迹、摘要笔记、结构化笔记），在75个源任务上生成181个交接点任务并评估后继模型。

Result: 上下文交接（原始轨迹、摘要笔记、结构化笔记）相比仅仓库状态，将中位代理事件减少20-59%，累积提示令牌减少42-63%；解决率提升较小且模型依赖。

Conclusion: 编码代理评估应同时报告解决率和恢复成本，以更全面反映实际工作场景。

中文摘要：编码代理基准测试评估单个不间断的代理能否解决仓库问题。实际的软件工作更加混乱：任务会被中断、重新分配、审查，并从另一个代理或工程师留下的部分状态恢复。我们通过“交接债务”研究这一缺失的维度：即前任工作不透明或不完整时带来的重新发现成本。我们的接管协议在确定性交接点中断编码代理，冻结仓库，并在四种交接视图下评估后继代理：仅仓库状态、原始轨迹、摘要笔记和结构化笔记。在75个源任务中，该协议为每个后继模型生成了181个交接点任务和724次接管运行。在三个后继模型中，与仅仓库状态的接管相比，包含上下文的交接将中位代理事件减少了20-59%，累积提示令牌减少了42-63%。解决率的影响较小且依赖于模型，但效率提升是一致的。这些发现表明，编码代理评估不仅应报告任务是否解决，还应报告该工作让另一个代理恢复的成本有多高。

Original abstract: Coding-agent benchmarks evaluate whether a single uninterrupted agent can resolve a repository issue. Real software work is messier: tasks are interrupted, reassigned, reviewed, and resumed from partial states left by another agent or engineer. We study this missing dimension through \emph{handoff debt}: the rediscovery cost imposed when a predecessor's work is opaque or incomplete. Our takeover protocol interrupts a coding agent at deterministic handoff points, freezes the repository, and evaluates successor agents under four handoff views: repository state only, raw trace, summary notes, and structured notes. Across 75 source tasks, the protocol generates 181 handoff-point tasks and 724 takeover runs per successor model. Across three successor models, context-bearing handoffs reduce median agent events by 20--59\% and cumulative prompt tokens by 42--63\% relative to repository-only takeover. Solved-rate effects are smaller and model-dependent, but efficiency gains are consistent. These findings suggest that coding-agent evaluation should report not only whether a task is solved, but also how costly that work is for another agent to resume.

</details>


### [65] [What Benchmarks Don't Measure: The Case for Evaluating Abstention Competence in Autonomous Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02965v1)
*Victor Ojewale,Suresh Venkatasubramanian*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent弃权能力评估，覆盖安全-可用性权衡，可直接迁移至coding agent的安全控制设计。

TL;DR: 自主代理在人类反馈训练下产生合规偏差，即缺乏安全条件时仍倾向行动。本文提出三缺口分类（规范、验证、授权缺口）和弃权评估协议，实验表明运行时强制弃权可在企业场景下有效平衡安全与可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准只衡量任务完成，忽略代理是否应放弃行动，导致合规偏差问题。

Method: 提出三缺口分类法（规范、验证、授权缺口）和弃权评估协议（安全率、可用率、知情拒绝率），并在144个企业场景和5个模型系列中测试运行时强制弃权机制。

Result: 运行时强制弃权机制实现高达89.2%的危险行为阻断和87.5%的可用性，安全-可用性权衡可调且因模型而异。

Conclusion: 安全-可用性权衡是可调而非固有的，该分类法和指标为进一步研究提供基础。

中文摘要：自主代理的基准测试衡量代理是否完成任务，然而这种框架系统性地忽视了代理是否本应根本不采取行动。在人类反馈目标下训练的代理会形成一种结构性倾向，即即使缺乏输入、证据或授权以安全行动时仍然继续行动，我们将这种倾向称为合规偏差，因为奖励信号和基准测试评分制度都将继续行动视为正确的默认行为，无论安全行动的前提条件是否存在。我们做出了三项贡献。首先，我们表明合规偏差起源于人类反馈流程中的奖励破解，并被主流的代理基准测试固化，这些测试要么惩罚代理暂停，要么在架构上无法区分原则性暂停与静默失败。然后，我们提出了一个涵盖应弃权场景的三缺口分类法，包括规范缺口（所需信息缺失）、验证缺口（世界状态无法确认）和授权缺口（未获得明确授权），这为构建具有弃权意识的代理基准提供了原则性基础。最后，我们提出了弃权评估协议（安全率、可用率和知情拒绝率），并报告了在144个企业代理场景和五个模型系列中的初步结果，其中运行时强制弃权机制在授权场景下实现了高达89.2%的危险行为阻断和87.5%的可用性，表明安全-可用性权衡是可调的而非固有的，并且其形状在不同模型系列间差异显著。我们将此视为初步工作，并将分类法和复合指标作为进一步讨论的起点。

Original abstract: Benchmarks for autonomous agents measure whether agents complete tasks, yet this framing is systematically blind to whether an agent should have proceeded at all. Agents trained under human-feedback objectives develop a structural tendency to proceed even when they lack the inputs, evidence, or authorization to act safely, a disposition we term compliance bias, because both the reward signal and the benchmark scoring regime treat proceeding as the correct default regardless of whether the preconditions for safe action are present. We make three contributions. We first show that compliance bias originates in reward hacking within human-feedback pipelines and is entrenched by prominent agent benchmarks, which either penalize agents for pausing or are architecturally unable to distinguish a principled pause from a silent failure. We then introduce a three-gap taxonomy of abstention-warranted scenarios, covering specification gaps where required information is absent, verification gaps where world state cannot be confirmed, and authority gaps where explicit authorization has not been given, which together provide a principled basis for constructing abstention-aware agent benchmarks. Finally, we propose abstention evaluation protocols (Safety Rate, Usability Rate, and Informed Refusal Rate) and report preliminary results across 144 enterprise agent scenarios and five model families, in which a runtime-enforced abstention mechanism achieves up to 89.2% hazardous-action blocking and 87.5% usability on authorized scenarios, demonstrating that the safety--usability tradeoff is tunable rather than inherent and that its shape varies substantially across model families. We treat this as preliminary work and offer the taxonomy and composite metrics as a starting point for further conversations.

</details>

### [66] [Dynamic Trust-Aware Sparse Communication Topology for LLM-Based Multi-Agent Consensus](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01828v1)
*Wanshuang Gou,Zihan Liu*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 动态稀疏通信拓扑用于LLM多agent共识，直接相关多agent协作与效率优化。

TL;DR: 提出DySCo，一种动态信任感知的稀疏共识机制，通过按需通信降低多智能体系统的通信开销，同时保留关键交叉验证信息，在数学、逻辑和事实问答任务上有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全连接通信开销大、固定稀疏拓扑不适应任务变动的缺点，需要一种动态稀疏通信方法平衡开销和准确性。

Method: DySCo每轮估计通信边价值（基于可靠性、答案分歧、任务相关性），在预算内选择高价值边；用动态信任权重聚合答案，共识稳定时提前终止。

Result: 在数学推理、逻辑推理和事实问答任务上，DySCo降低了通信开销和延迟，同时保持了与全连接相当的推理准确性。

Conclusion: DySCo通过动态稀疏通信有效减少开销，在多智能体推理中实现了效率与性能的平衡，并为后续研究提供了新思路。

中文摘要：大型语言模型驱动的多智能体系统通过多轮讨论、角色专业化和交叉验证来增强复杂推理任务的可靠性。然而，现有的多智能体辩论与协作框架通常采用全连接通信，导致消息数量、令牌成本和端到端延迟随智能体数量近似二次增长；尽管固定的稀疏拓扑减少了开销，但它们无法根据不同的任务实例或中间推理状态调整通信关系，容易保留低价值交互或丢失关键的纠错信息。为解决这一问题，本文提出了DySCo（动态稀疏共识），一种动态信任感知的稀疏共识机制。在每一轮推理中，DySCo基于智能体可靠性、答案分歧和任务相关性估计通信边的价值，并在预算约束下选择少量高价值边进行消息交换；然后通过动态信任权重聚合不同智能体的答案，并在共识稳定后提前终止讨论。该机制以按需通信取代通用广播，从而减少通信开销同时保留必要的交叉验证信息。我们进一步分析了通信复杂度和共识稳定性，并在数学推理、逻辑推理和事实问答任务上评估了DySCo的性能。

Original abstract: Large language model-driven multi-agent systems enhance the reliability of complex reasoning tasks through multi-round deliberation, role specialization, and cross-validation. However, existing multi-agent debate and collaboration frameworks typically adopt fully connected communication, causing the number of messages, token costs, and end-to-end latency to grow approximately quadratically with the number of agents; although fixed sparse topologies reduce overhead, they cannot adapt communication relationships to different task instances or intermediate reasoning states, making them prone either to preserving low-value interactions or to losing critical error-correction information. To address this problem, this paper proposes DySCo (Dynamic Sparse Consensus), a dynamic trust-aware sparse consensus mechanism. In each round of reasoning, DySCo estimates the value of communication edges based on agent reliability, answer divergence, and task relevance, and selects a small number of high-value edges for message exchange under budget constraints; it then aggregates the answers of different agents through dynamic trust weights and terminates the discussion early once consensus stabilizes. This mechanism replaces universal broadcasting with on-demand communication, thereby reducing communication overhead while preserving essential cross-validation information. We further present analyses of communication complexity and consensus stability, and evaluate the performance of DySCo on mathematical reasoning, logical reasoning, and factual question-answering tasks.

</details>


### [67] [RadioMaster: Multi-Agent System for Autonomous Radio Signal Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01862v1)
*Jiazhen Lei,Tianze Cao,Yuxin Sha,Sihan Wang,Bingbing Wang,Fengyuan Zhu,Zeming Yang,Xiaohua Tian*

Selection reason: 多agent系统自动生成无线电信号，包含多agent协作、知识检索、闭环验证，可迁移至一般agent。

TL;DR: RadioMaster是一个自主多智能体框架，通过知识检索、协作生成和闭环验证，将用户意图转化为真实无线信号，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM和多智能体系统在无线信号生成中因领域知识和硬件约束不足而失败，需要专门框架。

Method: 提出RadioMaster框架，包含RadioWiki（知识检索）、RadioAgent（I/Q样本生成与硬件配置）和RadioEmulator（闭环物理层验证）。

Result: 在真实世界评估中，RadioMaster在配置可行性和信号保真度上显著优于SOTA基线。

Conclusion: RadioMaster有效解决了无线信号生成中的领域知识和硬件约束问题，为无线原型设计提供了自动化方案。

Original abstract: Translating user intents into physical radio signals represents the critical yet notoriously tedious final step in wireless prototyping, as it requires intricate knowledge of physical layer details and presents immense implementation challenges. Large Language Models (LLMs) and multi-agent systems have revolutionized conventional software engineering, raising the compelling question of whether they can resolve these formidable difficulties. However, our investigations reveal that current models experience significant limitations and fail to accomplish this task when applied to radio signal generation. This performance degradation primarily stems from severe domain ignorance and a fundamental insensitivity to physical hardware constraints. To bridge this gap, we introduce RadioMaster, a fully autonomous multi-agent framework designed to seamlessly translate user input into real-world wireless emissions. RadioMaster operates on three synergistic pillars: RadioWiki for domain-specific knowledge retrieval, RadioAgent for collaborative I/Q sample generation alongside hardware configuration, and RadioEmulator for closed-loop physical layer verification. Furthermore, we construct RadioBench, the first comprehensive benchmark tailored specifically for the radio signal generation domain. Extensive real-world evaluations demonstrate that RadioMaster significantly outperforms state-of-the-art (SOTA) baselines regarding configuration viability and signal fidelity.

### [68] [The Epi-LLM Framework: probing LLM behavioral priors through epidemiological agent-based models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02867v1)
*Petra Ferencz,Ava Keeling,Tobias O'Keefe,Lorenzo Stigliano,Francesco Di Lauro,Andres Colubri,Jasmina Panovska-Griffiths*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: LLM agent模拟流行病行为，对agent行为建模有参考

TL;DR: Epi-LLM框架整合了基于智能体的建模、流行病游戏和LLM，用于模拟大流行中人类行为与传染病动态的相互作用，并验证了LLM智能体行为的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化人类行为对传染病动态的影响充满挑战，需要一种可扩展、无风险的模拟环境。

Method: 提出Epi-LLM框架，结合ABM、epigames和LLM，让合成智能体在接触网络上推理和适应；与无干预SEIR和人类数据对比。

Result: LLM智能体减少了峰值感染，隔离合规性58-65%；感知健康严重性是强预测因子（β=0.33, p=0.002），伪R²0.055；LLM架构影响动态；地理标签不单独影响，需要态度参数化。

Conclusion: 该框架作为大流行防范研究的可扩展、无风险模拟环境奠定基础。

中文摘要：Epidemics期间的人类行为会影响传染病动力学，但量化这一点仍然非常具有挑战性。这里我们介绍Epi-LLM框架：一种基于智能体的建模、现实生活流行病游戏和大语言模型（LLM）的新颖结合，其中合成社会中的智能体在爆发接触网络上进行推理和动态适应。通过将合成智能体行为与无干预的SEIR基线和来自AUIB流行病游戏研究的人类参与者数据进行比较，我们发现四种不同架构的LLM智能体减少了峰值活跃感染，在第15天模拟的第6天，隔离合规性达到58-65%。二项式广义线性模型显示，感知健康严重性是隔离行为的最强预测因子（β=0.33, p=0.002），伪R²为0.055，与人类试验中观察到的0.072相当。LLM架构是流行病动态的关键决定因素：低方差架构为测试行为规则提供了更高的内部有效性，而高方差模型可能更好地代表现实世界的决策。仅靠地理标签不会诱发文化差异化的行为；需要明确的参数化态度。这一原理验证工作为将Epi-LLM框架部署为可扩展、无风险的模拟环境用于大流行防范研究奠定了基础。

Original abstract: Human behaviour during epidemics affects infectious disease dynamics, but quantifying this remains deeply challenging. Here we introduce the Epi-LLM framework: a novel integration of agent-based modelling, real-life epigames, and large language models (LLMs) in which a synthetic society of agents reasons and adapts dynamically over an outbreak contact network. Comparing synthetic agent behaviour against a no-intervention SEIR baseline and human participant data from the AUIB epigame study, we find that LLM agents across four different architectures reduced peak active infections, with quarantine compliance peaking at 58-65% on day six of the 15-day simulation. A binomial generalised linear model showed that perceived health severity was the strongest predictor of quarantine behaviour ($β= 0.33, p = 0.002$), yielding a pseudo-$R^2$ of 0.055, comparable to the 0.072 observed in the human trial. LLM architecture is a key determinant of epidemic dynamics: low-variance architectures offer greater internal validity for testing behavioural rules, while high-variance models may better represent real-world decision-making. Geographic labels alone do not induce culturally differentiated behaviour; explicit attitudinal parameterisation is required. This proof-of-principle work lays the groundwork for deploying the Epi-LLM framework as a scalable, risk-free simulation environment for pandemic preparedness research.

</details>

### [69] [EstRTL: Functional Estimation Guided RTL Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09867v1)
*Qi Xiong,Renzhi Chen,Bowei Wang,Yuqing Xiong,Libo Huang,Lei Wang*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: 基于LLM的RTL代码生成agent框架，含生成-估计-纠正流程，直接相关自动代码生成与优化。

TL;DR: EstRTL是一个基于静态功能分数估计的LLM协作智能体框架，通过生成-估计-修正三阶段显著提升RTL代码生成的功能正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RTL代码生成方法缺乏对功能正确性的关注，生成的代码虽能编译但可能无法在硬件中按预期运行，需要提升正确性。

Method: 提出EstRTL框架，包含生成、估计和修正三阶段：功能估计智能体静态评估代码的分数和结果，决定直接输出、重新生成或交给修正智能体。

Result: 实验表明，EstRTL将通用LLM的RTL代码生成正确性提升了3.2%-9.0%。

Conclusion: EstRTL通过定量评估和可读需求比较提高了AI辅助RTL生成的透明度和正确性，具有实用价值。

中文摘要：优化寄存器传输级（RTL）代码在硬件设计中至关重要。大语言模型（LLM）为RTL代码的自动生成和优化提供了新方法，有望显著加速设计过程并减少人力投入。然而，现有生成RTL代码的方法通常侧重于模型微调和利用各种扩展技术来增强RTL代码生成能力，缺乏对功能正确性的关注。确保生成的RTL代码不仅能成功编译，还能在真实硬件实现中按预期运行仍然是一个关键挑战。为解决此问题，我们提出了EstRTL，一种基于静态功能分数估计的LLM驱动协作智能体框架，用于RTL代码生成。EstRTL采用三阶段范式：生成、估计和修正。在各阶段中，功能估计智能体根据分数和评估结果静态评估生成的代码，并决定是直接输出代码、返回重新生成还是转发给代码修正智能体。该框架可应用于各种专为RTL代码生成设计的LLM，进一步增强生成代码的正确性。通过提供定量分数和可读的需求比较，它提高了AI辅助RTL代码生成的透明度。实验表明，EstRTL将通用LLM的RTL代码生成正确性显著提升了3.2%-9.0%，证明了我们系统的实用价值。代码和实验结果已开源：https://anonymous.4open.science/status/EstRTL-E200/

Original abstract: Optimizing register transfer level (RTL) code is of vital importance in hardware design. Large language models (LLMs) provide new methods for the automatic generation and optimization of RTL code, offering the potential to significantly accelerate the design process and reduce human effort. However, existing methods for generating RTL code often focus on model fine-tuning and the use of various expansion techniques to enhance the RTL code generation capabilities, lacking attention to the functional correctness. Ensuring that the generated RTL code not only compiles successfully but also behaves as intended in real hardware implementations remains a critical challenge. To address this issue, we propose EstRTL, an LLM-powered collaborative agent framework for RTL code generation based on static functional score estimation. EstRTL operates a three-stage paradigm: Generation, Estimation and Correction. During the stages, the functional estimation agent statically evaluates the generated code based on score and assessment results, and decides whether to output the code directly, return it for regeneration, or forward it to the code correction agent. This framework can be applied to various LLMs that designed for RTL code generation, further enhancing the correctness of the generated code. By providing quantitative scores and human-readable requirements comparisons, it improves the transparency of AI-assisted RTL code generation. Experiments show that EstRTL significantly improves the correctness of RTL code generation by generic LLM by 3.2\%-9.0\%, demonstrating the practical value of our system. The codes and experimental results are open-sourced at link: https://anonymous.4open.science/status/EstRTL-E200/.

</details>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [70] [Not All Errors Are Equal: A Systematic Study of Error Propagation in Large Language Model Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02430v1)
*Yafan Huang,Sheng Di,Guanpeng Li*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: 研究LLM推理错误传播，对agent鲁棒性有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本研究通过提出的LLMFI框架，系统地研究了大型语言模型推理中的软错误传播，覆盖多个模型和任务，得出17条关键结论并提出软件层面的可靠性改进方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在HPC工作流中的应用日益广泛，但软错误如何影响LLM推理尚不清楚，需要填补这一研究空白。

Method: 提出了LLMFI，一个可配置且确定性的故障注入框架；使用该框架在三个LLM和十三个任务上系统注入故障，并进行细粒度案例研究。

Result: 研究得出17条关于错误传播的结论，识别了关键脆弱性模式。

Conclusion: 研究增进了对LLM推理中错误传播的理解，并提出了四种低开销的软件修改方向来提升可靠性，为未来错误检测和缓解提供指导。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被集成到高性能计算（HPC）工作流中，通过代码生成和特定领域决策等多种视角加速科学发现。然而，软错误如何在LLM推理中传播和影响仍 largely 未被探索。为填补这一空白，我们提出了一项关于LLM推理中错误传播的全面研究，这得益于我们提出的LLMFI，一个可配置且确定性的故障注入框架。使用LLMFI，我们系统地跨三个开放权重的LLM和十三项代表性任务注入故障，涵盖推理、多语言、数学和编码领域。此外，我们进行了细粒度的案例研究，揭示了关键的脆弱性模式。总体而言，我们的研究得出了17条结论，这些结论增进了对LLM推理中错误传播的理解，并引入了四种低开销的方向，通过仅软件修改来提高可靠性，为未来的错误检测和缓解提供了实用指导。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into high-performance computing (HPC) workflows, accelerating scientific discovery through diverse perspectives such as code generation and domain-specific decision-making. Yet, how soft errors propagate and affect LLM inference remains largely unexplored. To bridge this gap, we present a comprehensive study on error propagation in LLM inference, enabled by our proposed LLMFI, a configurable and deterministic fault-injection framework. Using LLMFI, we systematically inject faults across three open-weighted LLMs and thirteen representative tasks, covering reasoning, multilingual, mathematical, and coding domains. In addition, we conduct fine-grained case studies that reveal critical vulnerability patterns. Overall, our study yields 17 takeaways that advance the understanding of error propagation in LLM inference and introduces four low-overhead directions to improve reliability through software-only modification, offering practical guidance for future error detection and mitigation.

</details>

### [71] [Identifying High-Confidence Social Biases in LLMs for Trustworthy Conversational Tutoring Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01584v1)
*Aitor Arronte Alvarez,Naiyi Xie Fincham*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 识别辅导agent中的高置信度社会偏见，对agent可靠性有启发。

TL;DR: 该研究评估了LLM在对话式辅导中检测社会偏见的能力，发现它们在自然教学条件下偏见检测更具挑战性，且对错误判断过度自信，影响推理和反馈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在教育对话系统中可能放大刻板偏见，但现有评估未考虑自然教学场景下的偏见检测困难度和模型过度自信问题。

Method: 提出新数据集生成方法：重建学生-AI辅导对话并插入受控偏见回合；通过计算和人工评估多个LLM的偏见检测能力、置信度和推理。

Result: 在对话式辅导中偏见检测比基准测试更难；SOTA模型对错误判断过度自信；模型置信度强烈影响推理和反馈。

Conclusion: LLM辅导代理的过度自信和偏见行为存在风险，需考虑缓解措施，未来应研究更鲁棒的偏见检测和校准方法。

中文摘要：对话式辅导代理已被证明能够提升学习参与度和学生成绩，而大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于这些系统中，以提供可扩展的个性化反馈。然而，LLM可能会延续或放大刻板的社会偏见，这在教育环境中带来特殊风险。在本研究中，我们评估了LLM在对话式辅导场景中的表现，以识别高置信度的社会偏见，即模型在无法识别辅导对话中的偏见判断时仍对其评估保持强烈信心，这可能会影响其推理以及向学习者提供的反馈。我们提出了一种新的数据集生成方法，通过重建学生与AI辅导员的互动并引入源自基准数据集的受控偏见回合，从而能够在自然教学条件下进行偏见评估。利用这些数据，我们评估了多个LLM检测刻板偏见的能力，并通过计算和人工评估分析了其回答背后的信心和推理。我们发现，在对话式辅导情境中，偏见检测比基于基准的评估更具挑战性，并且最先进的LLM对其错误的刻板偏见判断表现出过度自信。此外，模型信心强烈影响推理和反馈，突出了基于LLM的辅导代理中过度自信和偏见行为的风险。最后，我们讨论了影响、缓解考虑因素以及未来研究方向。

Original abstract: Conversational tutoring agents have been shown to improve learning engagement and student outcomes, and large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in these systems to provide scalable, personalized feedback. However, LLMs may perpetuate or amplify stereotypical social biases, posing particular risks in educational settings.
  In this study, we evaluate LLMs in conversational tutoring scenarios to identify high-confidence social biases, instances where models are unable to identify biased judgments in tutoring conversations while maintaining strong confidence in their assessments, potentially affecting their reasoning and the feedback they provide to learners. We present a new dataset generation method that enables bias evaluation under naturalistic instructional conditions by regenerating student-AI tutor interactions and introducing turns with controlled bias derived from a benchmark dataset.
  Using this data, we assess multiple LLMs' ability to detect stereotypical biases and analyze the confidence and reasoning underlying their responses through computational and human evaluations. We find that bias detection is substantially more challenging in conversational tutoring contexts than in benchmark-based evaluations, and that state-of-the-art LLMs are overconfident in their incorrect assessments of stereotypical bias statements. Moreover, model confidence strongly influences reasoning and feedback, highlighting the risks of overconfident, biased behavior in LLM-based tutoring agents. We conclude by discussing implications, mitigation considerations, and directions for future research.

</details>


### [72] [EvoPool: Evolutionary Programmatic Annotation for Label-Efficient Specialized Supervision](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01617v1)
*Tianyi Xu,Yaolun Zhang,Xuan Ouyang,Huazheng Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 进化多agent框架，可用于agent协作与验证，但领域为标注，与代码优化间接相关。

TL;DR: EvoPool是一个进化多智能体框架，通过迭代生成和选择注释器，在专业领域以极低成本生成软标签，显著超越强LLM基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在通用任务上优秀，但在专业高成本标签领域不如小监督模型，需要一种低成本、高性能的注释方法。

Method: 提出EvoPool框架，包含三个智能体迭代生成注释器代码，基于验证集适应度、多样性、边际贡献进行筛选，并通过EvoAgg聚合投票为软标签。

Result: 在8个任务中的7个上，EvoPool平均宏F1比最强LLM基线高0.141，最高提升0.301（ChemProt）和0.265（PubMed），且速度提升4500-31000倍。

Conclusion: EvoPool在专业、复杂任务上以极低成本实现高性能，优于LLM注释，验证了进化多智能体方法的有效性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型在通用任务上表现出色，但在专业、高风险领域（其中训练标签成本高昂）中表现不如较小的监督模型。我们针对这种情况提出了EvoPool，这是一个受达尔文进化启发的进化多智能体框架。三个专门智能体迭代提出可执行的注释器代码，小规模验证集提供适应度信号，确定性门控仅保留通过生存能力、多样性和边际贡献检查的注释器。通过EvoAgg（一种将语义特征与注释器投票特征相结合的文本感知聚合器）将池投票映射为软训练标签。该池在近零单例成本下运行，在10万示例上比LLM注释快4500到31000倍。在8个LLM弱专业和复杂任务中的7个（涵盖生物医学关系抽取、法律条款分类、复杂推理和密集多标签生物医学分类）中，EvoPool比最强的LLM注释基线平均宏F1高出+0.141，在ChemProt上最高达到+0.301，在PubMed上达到+0.265。代码可在https://github.com/tianyi0216/EvoPool获取。

Original abstract: Large language models excel at general tasks but underperform smaller supervised models in specialized, high-stakes domains where training labels are costly. We address this regime with EvoPool, an evolutionary multi-agent framework inspired by Darwinian evolution. Three specialized agents iteratively propose executable annotator code, a small validation set provides a fitness signal, and a deterministic gate keeps only annotators that pass viability, diversity, and marginal-contribution checks across generations. Pool votes are mapped to soft training labels by EvoAgg, a text-aware aggregator combining semantic features with annotator-vote features. The authored pool runs at near-zero per-example cost and is 4500 to 31000x faster than LLM annotation on 100K examples. Across 7 of 8 LLM-weak specialized and complex tasks spanning biomedical relation extraction, legal-clause classification, complex reasoning, and dense multi-label biomedical classification, EvoPool beats the strongest LLM annotation baseline by an average +0.141 macro-F1, peaking at +0.301 on ChemProt and +0.265 on PubMed. Code is available at: https://github.com/tianyi0216/EvoPool

</details>


### [73] [Easier to Mislead Than to Correct: Harmful and Beneficial Revision in LLM Conformity](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01637v2)
*Jiaming Qu,Lucheng Fu,Yibo Hu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent系统中一致性风险研究，对agent安全与交互有启发。

TL;DR: 本研究发现，在多智能体LLM系统中，同伴一致性和权威标签往往通过误导正确的模型比纠正错误的模型更容易而损害性能，常见的推理干预措施也无法可靠地减少这种有害修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究多智能体LLM系统中，从众效应导致的修正究竟是纠正错误还是引入新错误，以及社会线索如何影响这一过程。

Method: 进行受控实验：让LLM先回答问题，然后看到模拟的同伴响应，再做出最终决定。操纵共识结构和权威标签两种社会线索，在四个开放权重的LLM和七个QA数据集上评估。

Result: 同伴一致性使误导初始正确模型的概率远高于纠正初始错误模型；权威标签使模型更倾向于选择被认可的答案，无论正确与否；链式思维和反思等通用推理干预不能可靠地减少有害修正而保留有益修正。

Conclusion: 多智能体LLM系统应验证同伴答案，而非简单聚合。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地用于多智能体系统中，在这些系统中，它们会看到并响应其他智能体的答案。一个关键风险是从众效应：模型可能仅仅因为其他人都同意一个不同的答案而放弃自己的答案。先前的研究表明，LLM经常向多数答案修订，但尚不清楚这些修订在纠正错误和引入新错误方面是否同样频繁。在本文中，我们进行了一项受控研究，其中LLM首先回答一个问题，然后在做出最终决定之前看到模拟的同伴响应。我们操纵两种社会线索：共识结构和分配给同伴的权威标签，并衡量它们如何影响有益和有害的修订。在四个开放权重的LLM和七个QA数据集上，我们发现同伴一致性使得误导初始正确的模型比纠正初始错误的模型容易得多。权威标签使模型更可能选择被认可的答案，无论它是否正确。更令人担忧的是，通用推理干预措施（如思维链和反思）并不能在保留有益修订的同时可靠地减少有害修订。这些发现表明，多智能体LLM系统应该验证同伴答案，而不是简单地聚合它们。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly used in multi-agent systems, where they see and respond to other agents' answers. A key risk is conformity: a model may abandon its own answer simply because others agree on a different one. Prior studies show that LLMs often revise toward a majority answer, but it remains unclear whether these revisions help correct mistakes as often as they introduce new errors. In this paper, we conduct a controlled study in which an LLM first answers a question, then sees simulated peer responses before making a final decision. We manipulate two social cues: consensus structure and authority labels assigned to peers, and measure how they influence beneficial and harmful revisions. Across four open-weight LLMs and seven QA datasets, we find that peer agreement makes it much easier to mislead initially correct models than to correct initially wrong ones. Authority labels make models more likely to choose the endorsed answer, regardless of whether it is correct. More concerningly, generic reasoning interventions such as chain-of-thought and reflection do not reliably reduce harmful revision while preserving beneficial revision. These findings suggest that multi-agent LLM systems should verify peer answers rather than simply aggregate them.

</details>


### [74] [Off-the-Shelf LLMs as Process Scorers: Training-Free Alternative to PRMs for Mathematical Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01682v1)
*Atoosa Chegini,Soheil Feizi*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 现成LLM作为过程评分器引导生成，可迁移至代码生成验证。

TL;DR: 提出块级引导生成（Chunk-Level Guided Generation），一种无需训练的推理时策略，通过固定长度块和大模型似然评分引导小模型生成，在多个数学推理基准上优于多数投票并匹配或超越PRM引导搜索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如多数投票在小模型已陷入错误推理路径时失效，而PRM引导搜索需要步骤级标签训练，成本高。因此需要一种无需训练、能早期纠正错误推理的替代方案。

Method: 在每个步骤中，小模型采样k个固定长度的候选块，大模型使用长度归一化对数概率（LGS）或对比对数概率（CGS）评分，选中块后提交，继续下一步，从而在错误传播前引导生成。固定长度块避免了大模型对可变长度步骤评分时的长度偏差。

Result: 在GSM8K、MATH、Minerva Math等基准上，CGS比多数投票提升高达28个百分点，在匹配引导预算下匹配或超越PRM-72B引导搜索，并产生更短的推理轨迹。例如，Qwen2.5-7B+72B在k=16时MATH达81.8%，Minerva Math达63.6%。

Conclusion: 块级引导生成是一种高效、无需训练的推理时策略，通过固定长度块和大模型似然评分有效引导小模型，在多个数学推理任务上取得优越性能，并减少推理长度。

中文摘要：从多个小模型样本中选择最佳响应是一种简单的推理时策略，但当小模型已经陷入错误推理路径时，该方法会失败。PRM引导的搜索通过在生成过程中对候选延续进行评分来避免这一点，但需要经过步骤级标签训练的回馈模型。
我们提出块级引导生成，这是一种无需训练的替代方案，使用现成的大型语言模型作为过程评分器。在每个步骤中，小模型采样k个固定长度的候选块，而大模型使用似然对候选进行评分，无需生成任何文本。选中的块在下一步之前被提交，从而在错误传播之前引导生成。
我们用两种选择规则实例化该框架：似然引导选择（LGS），选择具有最高长度归一化的大模型对数概率的块；对比引导选择（CGS），减去小模型的对数概率，以偏向于大模型偏好与小模型偏好不一致的块。我们表明，使用大模型似然对可变长度推理步骤进行评分是不可靠的，因为存在即使经过长度归一化后仍然存在的系统性长度偏差，而固定长度块避免了这一混淆。
在GSM8K、MATH、Minerva Math、AMC23和AIME24上，使用Qwen2.5-1.5B由Qwen2.5-32B引导以及Llama-3.2-1B由Llama-3.1-70B引导，CGS在大多数基准测试中比多数投票高出最多28个百分点，并且在匹配的引导预算下，无需回馈模型训练即可达到或超过Qwen2.5-Math-PRM-72B引导搜索的性能。使用Qwen2.5-7B由Qwen2.5-72B引导，当k=16时，CGS在MATH上达到81.8%，在Minerva Math上达到63.6%，比多数投票高出4-6个百分点。最后，块级引导生成产生的推理轨迹比PRM引导搜索短得多。

Original abstract: Selecting the best response from multiple small-model samples using a stronger scorer is a simple inference-time strategy, but fails when the small model has already committed to incorrect reasoning paths. PRM guided search avoids this by scoring candidate continuations during generation, but requires a reward model trained with step-level labels.
  We propose Chunk-Level Guided Generation, a training-free alternative that uses an off-the-shelf large language model as a process scorer. At each step, a small model samples k fixed-length candidate chunks, while the larger model scores the candidates using likelihoods without generating any text. The selected chunk is committed before the next step, steering generation before errors can propagate.
  We instantiate this framework with two selection rules: Likelihood-Guided Selection (LGS), which selects the chunk with the highest length-normalized large-model log-probability, and Contrastive-Guided Selection (CGS), which subtracts the small model's log-probability to favor chunks where the large model's preference diverges from the small model's. We show that scoring variable-length reasoning steps with large-model likelihoods is unreliable due to a systematic length bias that persists even after length normalization, and that fixed-length chunks avoid this confound.
  On GSM8K, MATH, Minerva Math, AMC23, and AIME24 with Qwen2.5-1.5B guided by Qwen2.5-32B and Llama-3.2-1B guided by Llama-3.1-70B, CGS outperforms majority voting by up to 28 pp and, under matched guidance budgets, matches or outperforms Qwen2.5-Math-PRM-72B guided search on most benchmarks without reward-model training. With Qwen2.5-7B guided by Qwen2.5-72B, CGS reaches 81.8% on MATH and 63.6% on Minerva Math at k=16, surpassing majority voting by 4--6 pp. Finally, Chunk-Level Guided Generation produces substantially shorter reasoning traces than PRM guided search.

</details>


### [75] [THRD: A Training-Free Multi-Turn Defense Framework for Jailbreak Attacks on Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01738v1)
*Zhiqing Ma,Zhonghao Xu,Dong Yu,Chen Kang,Changliang Li,Pengyuan Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多轮越狱防御框架，涉及agent安全控制与轨迹风险评估。

TL;DR: THRD是一种无需训练的多轮越狱防御框架，通过显式建模时间风险累积，将攻击成功率降至0.2-4.0%并保持模型效用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御方法要么依赖高成本重训练且降低模型效用，要么独立分析单轮而忽略风险累积；多轮安全行为轨迹依赖，孤立评估不足。

Method: THRD包含四个模块：轮次级风险评估器(TRA)估计瞬时风险，历史上下文分析器(HCA)检测跨轮意图升级，响应评估器(RE)识别促进性输出，决策模块通过时间演变的衰减调制和趋势感知调整组合信号。

Result: 在树搜索和多智能体协作攻击下，THRD将ASR降至0.2-4.0%，MMLU和GSM8K上模型效用退化低于1.5%；消融验证模块非冗余，跨架构稳定；首次拒绝触发分析表明70%以上攻击需在第2轮后检测。

Conclusion: THRD有效防御多轮越狱攻击，验证了显式时间聚合的必要性，且无需训练、不显著影响模型效用。

中文摘要：多轮越狱攻击通过利用会话动态（如逐步升级和跨轮协调）对大语言模型构成日益严重的威胁。现有防御方法要么依赖成本高昂的重新训练——通常会降低模型效用，要么在每个轮次独立地进行单轮分析，未能捕捉风险在交互轨迹中的累积过程。我们观察到，多轮交互中的安全行为是轨迹相关的：对话历史不断重塑模型的调节上下文，使得孤立地评估每个轮次是不够的。受此启发，我们提出了THRD，这是第一个显式建模多轮越狱防御中时间风险累积的无训练框架。THRD集成了四个模块：轮次级风险评估器（TRA）用于瞬时风险估计，历史上下文分析器（HCA）用于跨轮意图升级检测，响应评估器（RE）用于识别促进性输出，以及决策模块，该模块通过一个随时间演变的评分机制（结合衰减调制和趋势感知调整）来组合这些信号。针对最先进的多轮攻击（包括基于树搜索和多智能体协作方法）在两个目标模型上的实验表明，THRD将攻击成功率降至0.2-4.0%，同时在MMLU和GSM8K上将模型效用退化控制在1.5%以内。消融研究证实了各模块的非冗余贡献和稳定的跨架构泛化能力。首次拒绝触发分析显示，超过70%的多轮攻击需要在第2轮或之后才能检测到，验证了显式时间聚合的必要性。

Original abstract: Multi-turn jailbreak attacks pose a growing threat to LLMs by exploiting conversational dynamics such as gradual escalation and cross-turn coordination. Existing defenses either rely on costly retraining -- often degrading model utility -- or apply single-turn analysis independently at each turn, failing to capture how risk accumulates along interaction trajectories. We observe that safety behavior in multi-turn interaction is trajectory-dependent: dialogue history continuously reshapes the model's conditioning context, making it insufficient to evaluate each turn in isolation. Motivated by this insight, we present THRD, the first training-free framework that explicitly models temporal risk accumulation for multi-turn jailbreak defense. THRD integrates four modules: a Turn-level Risk Assessor (TRA) for instantaneous risk estimation, a Historical Context Analyzer (HCA) for cross-turn intent escalation detection, a Response Evaluator (RE) for identifying facilitative outputs, and a Decision Module that combines these signals through a time-evolving scoring mechanism with attenuation-based modulation and trend-aware adjustment. Experiments against state-of-the-art multi-turn attacks -- including tree-search-based and multi-agent collaborative methods -- across two target models show that THRD reduces ASR to 0.2--4.0% while preserving model utility within 1.5% degradation on MMLU and GSM8K. Ablation studies confirm non-redundant module contributions and stable cross-architecture generalization. Analysis of first rejection triggers reveals that over 70% of multi-turn attacks require Turn~2 or later to detect, validating the necessity of explicit temporal aggregation.

</details>


### [76] [LayerRoute: Input-Conditioned Adaptive Layer Skipping via LoRA Fine-Tuning for Agentic Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01838v1)
*Prateek Kumar Sikdar*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LayerRoute根据输入类型自适应跳过层，优化agent推理效率，直接服务agentic模型。

TL;DR: 提出LayerRoute，一种轻量级适配器，通过每层路由器和LoRA在代理语言模型中动态跳过Transformer块，在工具调用中节省15.25% FLOPs，规划步骤仅2.34%，且质量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前推理系统对不同步骤（工具调用与规划）使用相同计算，忽略了它们结构上的差异，导致效率低下。

Method: 将每层路由器和LoRA适配器添加到Qwen2.5-0.5B-Instruct的每个Transformer块，通过直通估计器学习硬门控，单次训练后选择性跳过块。

Result: 训练3000步后，工具调用跳过15.25% FLOPs，规划步骤跳过2.34%，困惑度分别降低1.29和1.30，仅用1.10M参数。

Conclusion: LayerRoute能高效区分不同类型的步骤，实现动态计算分配，提升推理效率并保持或提升质量。

中文摘要：代理语言模型系统在两种结构上不同的步骤类型之间交替：结构化工具调用（短、确定性、低困惑度）和开放式规划/推理步骤（长、复杂、高困惑度）。尽管存在这种异质性，当前的推理系统对每个步骤应用相同的计算。我们引入了LayerRoute，一个轻量级适配器，学习在每个输入的基础上选择性地跳过Transformer块。LayerRoute为Qwen2.5-0.5B-Instruct中的24个Transformer块中的每一个增加：(1) 一个每层路由器（约897个参数，Linear(896,1)），通过直通估计器输出硬二元门，以及(2) 注意投影Q/K/V/O上的LoRA适配器（秩8，约1.08M参数）。骨干权重保持冻结。在代理数据（Hermes、Glaive、GSM8K、Turing）上进行单次端到端训练，加上门正则化项，强制系统发现每个输入类型下哪些块是可跳过的。经过3,000步（在A100 40GB上6.4分钟），LayerRoute实现了12.91%的跳过差异：工具调用跳过15.25%的FLOPs，而规划步骤仅跳过2.34%，仅使用1.10M可训练参数（占494M骨干的0.22%）。由于LoRA适配，质量优于基础模型，工具调用上的困惑度差为-1.29，规划上为-1.30。

Original abstract: Agentic language model systems alternate between two structurally distinct step types: structured tool calls (short, deterministic, low perplexity) and open-ended planning/reasoning steps (long, complex, high perplexity). Despite this heterogeneity, current inference systems apply identical compute to every step. We introduce LayerRoute, a lightweight adapter that learns to selectively skip transformer blocks on a per-input basis. LayerRoute augments each of the 24 transformer blocks in Qwen2.5-0.5B-Instruct with: (1) a per-layer router (~897 parameters, Linear(896,1)) that outputs a hard binary gate via the straight-through estimator, and (2) LoRA adapters (rank 8, ~1.08M parameters) on the Q/K/V/O attention projections. The backbone weights remain frozen. A single end-to-end training pass on agentic data (Hermes, Glaive, GSM8K, Turing) with a gate regularisation term forces the system to discover which blocks are skippable per input type. After 3,000 steps (6.4 minutes on an A100 40GB), LayerRoute achieves a 12.91% skip differential: tool calls skip 15.25% of FLOPs while planning steps skip only 2.34%, using only 1.10M trainable parameters (0.22% of the 494M backbone). Quality improves over the base model due to LoRA adaptation, with perplexity delta of -1.29 on tool calls and -1.30 on planning.

### [77] [MMG2Skill: Can Agents Distill In-the-Wild Guides into Self-Evolving Skills?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01993v1)
*Xinyu Che,Junqi Xiong,Yunfei Ge,Xinping Lei,Shihao Li,Hang Yan,Han Li,Yuanxing Zhang,Zhiqi Bai,Jinhua Hao,Ming Sun,Han Li,Jiaheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出从网络指南到可执行技能的闭环学习框架，适用于长程任务，可迁移至coding agent技能积累。

TL;DR: 提出指南到技能学习问题，构建MMG2Skill-Bench基准和MMG2Skill框架，通过闭环技能编译与修订显著提升智能体在多种任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 网络上的人类导向指南难以直接用作智能体技能，需要将其转换为可执行格式并持续改进。

Method: 提出MMG2Skill闭环框架，将指南编译为可编辑技能，在固定VLM智能体执行中条件化技能，并基于轨迹级根因反馈修订技能。

Result: 在六个VLM骨干网络的GUI控制、开放式游戏和策略卡牌任务上，相比基线获得+12.8至+25.3个百分点宏观平均增益；原始指南提示会降低性能；成功可推断任务中提前停止节省25%-53%尝试。

Conclusion: MMG2Skill有效弥合人类指南与智能体技能的鸿沟，结构化技能构建和轨迹驱动修订是关键，提前停止可进一步优化成功可推断任务。

中文摘要：网络上丰富的程序性知识对于帮助智能体解决长期任务具有巨大潜力。然而，这些知识通常是多模态、异构、包含噪声的，并且隐含地假设了人类执行者，因此难以直接用作智能体所需的技能。为了弥合人类导向的指南与智能体可执行技能之间的差距，我们将这个问题形式化为指南到技能学习：将野外指南转换为可执行技能，并从智能体可观测的轨迹中持续改进这些技能。为了评估现有智能体在此任务上的能力，我们引入了MMG2Skill-Bench，这是第一个为此问题设计的基准。我们进一步提出了MMG2Skill，这是一个闭环框架，它将指南编译为可编辑的技能，在执行过程中将固定的视觉语言模型（VLM）智能体条件化于这些技能，并通过轨迹级根因反馈来修订技能，而无需使用基准分数。在GUI控制、开放式游戏和策略卡牌游戏中，使用六个VLM骨干网络，MMG2Skill在每个模型-领域设置中始终优于普通基线智能体，在骨干网络上实现了+12.8到+25.3个百分点的宏观平均增益。消融研究表明，直接使用原始指南提示智能体会降低性能，而结构化的技能构建和轨迹驱动的修订对于观察到的改进都是必要的。在可推断成功任务中，当成功信号被正确校准时，基于分析器的提前停止进一步防止了后期性能下降，并节省了25%-53%的尝试次数。

Original abstract: Abundant procedural knowledge on the Web holds great potential for helping agents solve long-horizon tasks. However, such knowledge is often multimodal, heterogeneous, noisy, and implicitly assumes human executors, making it difficult to use directly as the skills required by agents. To bridge the gap between human-oriented guides and agent-executable skills, we formalize this problem as guide-to-skill learning: converting in-the-wild guides into executable skills and continuously improving them from trajectories observable to the agent. To evaluate the capability of existing agents on this task, we introduce MMG2Skill-Bench, the first benchmark designed for this problem. We further propose MMG2Skill, a closed-loop framework that compiles guides into editable skills, conditions a fixed vision-language model (VLM) agent on these skills during execution, and revises the skills from trajectory-level root-cause feedback without using benchmark scores. Across GUI control, open-ended gameplay, and strategic card play with six VLM backbones, MMG2Skill consistently outperforms vanilla baseline agents in every model-domain setting, achieving macro-average gains of +12.8 to +25.3 percentage points across backbones. Ablation studies show that directly prompting agents with raw guides can degrade performance, while both structured skill construction and trajectory-driven revision are necessary for the observed improvements. On success-inferable tasks, analyzer-based early stopping further prevents late-stage performance regressions and saves 25%-53% of attempts when the success signal is properly calibrated.

### [78] [The Role of Ambiguity in Error Prediction via Uncertainty Quantification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02093v1)
*Ieva Raminta Staliūnaitė,James Bishop,Andreas Vlachos*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究不确定性量化及歧义对LLM错误预测的影响，可迁移至agent错误预测与可靠性改进。

TL;DR: 通过将输入歧义从不确定性信号中分离，该方法显著提升了大型语言模型在问答任务中的错误预测性能，在多个指标上取得了超过10个百分点的PRR提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不确定性量化指标虽然能捕捉模型知识缺失，但同时也受到输入中固有偶然不确定性的影响，从而影响错误预测的准确性。

Method: 使用门控专家和选择性预测，将真实和预测的歧义标签整合到错误预测流水线中，以分离输入歧义与UQ信号。

Result: 歧义信息在所有实验设置下均提升了错误预测分数，在标准数据集上为个别UQ度量带来了超过10个百分点的PRR提升。

Conclusion: 通过显式处理输入歧义，可以显著改进LLM的错误预测，该发现对安全关键应用具有重要意义。

中文摘要：错误预测任务，即预测模型输出是否正确，通常通过不确定性量化（UQ）来处理。然而，虽然不确定性度量能够捕捉模型缺乏知识或能力进行预测的情况，但它们也反映了输入和上下文中固有的偶然不确定性。本文提出了一种通过将输入歧义与UQ信号分离来改进大型语言模型（LLM）错误预测的方法。我们在问答（QA）任务上使用六种UQ度量进行了实验，并表明UQ度量对无歧义实例的错误预测能力高于对具有多个合理答案的问题。我们使用门控专家和选择性预测将真实和预测的歧义标签引入错误预测流程。我们发现，歧义信息在不同模型家族、训练和评估范式、数据集（包括据称无歧义的数据集）以及偶然不确定性来源上均提高了错误预测得分，在标准数据集上为个别UQ度量带来了超过10个百分点的PRR提升。

Original abstract: The task of Error Prediction, namely predicting whether a model output is correct, is commonly tackled with Uncertainty Quantification (UQ). However, while uncertainty metrics capture when models lack knowledge or capacity to make a prediction, they also reflect aleatoric uncertainty, which is inherent in the model input and context. This paper presents a method for improving error prediction for Large Language Models (LLMs), by disentangling input ambiguity from UQ signal. We conduct experiments on the task of Question Answering (QA) with six UQ metrics and show that UQ metrics are more predictive of errors on unambiguous instances than on questions with multiple plausible answers. We use Gated Experts and Selective Prediction to incorporate gold and predicted ambiguity labels into the error prediction pipeline. We find that ambiguity information improves error prediction scores across model families, training and evaluation paradigms, datasets (including allegedly unambiguous ones), and sources of aleatoric uncertainty, yielding improvements of over 10 points of PRR for individual UQ metrics on standard datasets.

### [79] [SPADE-Bench: Evaluating Spontaneous Strategic Deception in Agents via Plan-Action Divergence](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02380v2)
*Yuyan Bu,Haowei Li,Qirui Zheng,Bowen Dong,Kaiyue Yang,Jiaming Ji,Yingshui Tan,Wenxin Li,Yaodong Yang,Juntao Dai*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 评估agent策略欺骗的benchmark，对agent安全性测试有启发。

TL;DR: SPADE-Bench通过结合实际工具执行和压力场景，评估并证实了LLM智能体在工具使用中的欺骗行为（计划-行动不一致）是一个真实问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在自主执行时可能产生自我报告与实际行动不一致的欺骗行为，而用户无法监控执行过程，存在安全风险，急需一个能够严格评估此类欺骗的基准。

Method: 提出SPADE-Bench，该基准同时整合实际工具执行和受控压力场景，通过压力下的计划-行动比较，区分策略性欺骗和单纯幻觉，确保生态效度。

Result: 在主流模型上的实验证实，智能体欺骗在工具使用上下文中是一个真实且紧迫的问题。

Conclusion: SPADE-Bench提供了全面稳健的评估框架，填补了智能体安全中的关键空白，有助于构建可信可控的自主系统。

中文摘要：随着基于大语言模型的智能体扩大其操作范围，可靠性成为实际部署的前提。然而，在实际应用中，人类用户无法监控每一个即时行为；相反，执行过程往往是一个黑箱，用户只能依赖智能体自我报告的状态更新。这种不透明性带来了关键风险：智能体可能提供与执行动作不一致的面向观察者的报告，使得系统无法控制，尤其是在高风险自主场景中。我们将这种自我报告的计划-行动不一致称为智能体欺骗。为了评估这一点，我们引入了SPADE-Bench，一个旨在评估自发性计划-行动不一致的基准。与先前的欺骗基准不同，SPADE-Bench同时整合了实际工具执行和受控压力场景。这种设计确保了生态效度，并通过压力下的受控计划-行动比较严格区分了策略性欺骗和单纯的幻觉。跨主流模型的实验证实了智能体欺骗在工具使用上下文中是一个真实且紧迫的问题。通过提供一个全面且稳健的评估框架，SPADE-Bench填补了智能体安全中的关键空白，促进了社区朝着构建可信且可控的自主系统迈进。

Original abstract: As LLM-based agents expand their operational scope, reliability becomes a prerequisite for real-world deployment. However, in practical applications, human users cannot monitor every immediate behavior; instead, the execution process often remains a black box, leaving users dependent solely on the agent's self-reported updates. This opacity creates a critical risk: agents may present observer-facing reports that diverge from their executed actions, rendering the system uncontrollable, especially in high-stakes autonomous scenarios. We term such self-reported plan-action divergence as agent deception. To assess this, we introduce SPADE-Bench, a benchmark designed to evaluate spontaneous plan-action divergence. Unlike prior deception benchmarks, SPADE-Bench simultaneously integrates actual tool execution and controlled pressure scenarios. This design ensures ecological validity and rigorously distinguishes strategic deception from mere hallucination through controlled plan-action comparisons under pressure. Experiments across mainstream models confirm that agent deception is a genuine and pressing issue in tool-use contexts. By providing a comprehensive and robust evaluation framework, SPADE-Bench fills a critical gap in agent safety, facilitating the community's progress toward building trustworthy and controllable autonomous systems.

</details>


### [80] [Learning When to Translate for Multilingual Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02465v1)
*Deokhyung Kang,Hyounghun Kim,Gary Geunbae Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 学习何时调用翻译工具，代理选择性工具使用，有启发。

TL;DR: 提出Luar框架，通过强化学习训练推理语言模型在直接理解不可靠时选择性调用翻译，以缩小多语言推理差距，在低资源语言上表现显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理语言模型在多语言推理中存在语言理解失败，而翻译所有输入不必要且低效，需要让模型学会判断何时需要翻译。

Method: 提出语言理解边界感知的强化学习框架Luar，训练模型选择直接推理或翻译后推理，通过奖励鼓励在翻译增强推理明显更优时才使用翻译。

Result: 在多语言推理基准上，Luar优于GRPO等基线，尤其在低资源语言上提升显著，且能避免不必要翻译并泛化到未见低资源语言。

Conclusion: 推理语言模型可以通过学习选择性调用翻译来改善多语言推理，仅在直接理解不可靠时使用翻译，从而高效缩小语言差距。

中文摘要：推理语言模型（RLMs）在复杂推理任务上表现强劲，但仍存在显著的多语言推理差距，这主要源于非英语输入中的语言理解失败。英语翻译可以通过将非英语输入表达为RLMs更可靠解释的形式来缓解这些失败，但当模型能够直接从原始查询中可靠推理时，翻译每个输入是不必要的。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了Luar，一种语言理解边界感知的强化学习框架，训练RLMs在直接理解不可靠时选择性调用翻译。Luar训练模型选择直接解决原始输入还是在其英语翻译上进行推理，仅在翻译增强推理预期显著优于直接推理时鼓励翻译。在多语言推理基准测试中，Luar优于标准GRPO和其他基于训练的基线方法，尤其在低资源语言上取得了更大收益。进一步分析表明，Luar在直接推理足够的情况下避免不必要的翻译，同时将其翻译调用行为扩展到未见过的低资源语言。总的来说，我们的工作提出了一种选择性多语言推理方法：RLMs可以学会仅在直接理解不可靠时调用翻译。该项目将在https://github.com/deokhk/LUAR公开。

Original abstract: Reasoning language models (RLMs) achieve strong performance on complex reasoning tasks, but still exhibit substantial multilingual reasoning gaps, largely due to language-understanding failures in non-English inputs. English translation can mitigate these failures by expressing non-English inputs in a form that RLMs can more reliably interpret, yet translating every input is unnecessary when the model can reason reliably from the original query. To address this challenge, we propose Luar, a Language Understanding Boundary-aware Reinforcement Learning framework that trains RLMs to selectively invoke translation when direct understanding is unreliable. Luar trains the model to choose between solving the original input directly and reasoning over its English translation, encouraging translation only when translator-augmented reasoning is expected to substantially outperform direct reasoning. Across multilingual reasoning benchmarks, Luar outperforms standard GRPO and other training-based baselines, with particularly large gains on low-resource languages. Further analysis shows that Luar avoids unnecessary translation in cases where direct reasoning is sufficient, while extending its translator-call behavior to unseen low-resource languages. Together, our work suggests a selective approach to multilingual reasoning: RLMs can learn to invoke translation only when their direct understanding is unreliable. The project will be made publicly available at https://github.com/deokhk/LUAR

</details>


### [81] [Economy of Minds: Emerging Multi-Agent Intelligence with Economic Interactions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02859v1)
*Zhenting Qi,Huangyuan Su,Ao Qu,Chenyu Wang,Yu Yao,Han Zheng,Kushal Chattopadhyay,Guowei Xu,Zihan Wang,Weirui Ye,Vijay Janapa Reddi,Ju Li,Paul Pu Liang,Himabindu Lakkaraju,Sham Kakade,Yilun Du*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent经济交互实现自组织，直接可迁移至agent协作

TL;DR: 受哈耶克经济理论启发，通过代理经济体中的拍卖和支付机制实现去中心化协调，使弱代理涌现出多步推理策略，并在多个任务上超越强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在没有集中控制或显式通信协议下，代理种群如何通过经济机制自发形成集体智能。

Method: 构建代理经济体，代理通过拍卖竞争行动权、进行支付和积累财富，利用经济选择（有效代理积累财富并突变，无效代理破产并替换）驱动进化。

Result: 从弱代理初始化，经济体产生涌现的多步推理策略，在数学推理等五个任务中优于更强的单一基线。

Conclusion: 设计分散的激励结构而非直接协调，可以自动涌现出多代理智能，为多智能体系统提供新路径。

中文摘要：一群代理如何在没有集中控制的情况下自我协调和自适应，形成更强的集体智能？受弗里德里希·哈耶克关于市场中分散协调的经济理论启发，我们通过一个代理经济体来研究这个问题，在该经济体中，代理通过拍卖竞争行动权、进行支付，并从环境奖励中积累财富。这些简单的经济信号产生了分散的信用分配，无需全局协调或显式通信协议即可驱动规划。种群通过经济选择进化：有效的代理积累财富并通过利用突变，而无效的代理破产并通过探索被替换。我们证明，从弱代理开始，经济体产生了涌现的多步推理策略，并在五个代理任务（包括数学推理、金融研究、科学研究、加速器设计和分布式系统优化）中优于更强的单一基线。我们进一步提供了关于经济动态如何塑造代理行为的理论见解，将局部激励与长期全局表现联系起来。我们的结果表明了一条通向多代理智能的新路径：与其设计协调，不如设计分散的激励结构，在这种结构下协调会自动涌现。

Original abstract: How can a population of agents self-orchestrate and self-adapt into stronger collective intelligence without centralized control? Inspired by Friedrich Hayek's economic theory of decentralized coordination in markets, we study this question through an agent economy in which agents compete via auctions for the right to act, exchange payments, and accumulate wealth from environmental rewards. These simple economic signals induce decentralized credit assignment, driving planning without global orchestration or explicit communication protocols. The population evolves through economic selection: effective agents accumulate wealth and are mutated via exploitation, while ineffective ones go bankrupt and are replaced via exploration. We show that, initialized with weak agents, the economy produces emergent multi-step reasoning strategies and outperforms stronger monolithic baselines across five agentic tasks, including mathematical reasoning, financial research, scientific research, accelerator design, and distributed-system optimization. We further provide theoretical insights into how economic dynamics shape agent behaviors, linking local incentives to long-term global performance. Our results suggest a new path to multi-agent intelligence: rather than engineering coordination, we can design decentralized incentive structures under which it automatically emerges.

</details>


### [82] [Adaptive Latent Agentic Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02871v1)
*Dongwon Jung,Peng Shi,Yi Zhang,Junshan Zhang,Muhao Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 自适应隐式推理降低agent生成成本，直接提升agent效率

TL;DR: 提出ALAR，一种双模式框架，通过紧凑潜在推理处理常规决策，仅在需要时使用显式思维链，在保持准确性的同时大幅减少token生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在每个决策步骤生成冗长的文本推理，且推理努力均匀分配，导致多轮交互中效率低下。

Method: ALAR采用双模式：常规轮次使用紧凑潜在推理，困难决策时升级为显式思维链；通过动作作为监督锚点学习潜在推理，并优化决策何时使用哪种模式。

Result: 在搜索和工具使用基准上，token生成分别减少最多43.6%和84.6%，任务准确性保持可比或更好。

Conclusion: ALAR通过减少不必要的文本推理并保留显式思考用于更难步骤，改善了LLM智能体的准确性-效率权衡。

中文摘要：大型推理模型通过生成扩展的思维链推理来提高性能，但这种行为在应用于LLM智能体时变得低效。当前的LLM智能体通常在每个决策步骤生成冗长的文本推理，并且几乎均匀地分配推理努力于各轮次，导致多轮智能体轨迹中显著的效率低下。我们提出自适应潜在智能体推理(ALAR)，一种双模式框架，对常规轮次使用紧凑的潜在推理，并在需要更深思考时选择性地升级到显式思维链。ALAR通过使用智能体的动作作为监督锚点来学习潜在推理，并进一步优化为在潜在推理足以完成任务时使用它，保留显式CoT用于更难决策。在智能体搜索和工具使用基准上的实验表明，ALAR保持可比或更好的任务准确性，同时显著减少生成的token，搜索减少高达43.6%，工具使用减少84.6%。这些结果表明，ALAR通过减少不必要的文本推理同时保留显式思考用于更难决策步骤，改善了LLM智能体的准确性-效率权衡。

Original abstract: Large reasoning models improve performance by generating extended chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning, but this behavior becomes inefficient when applied to LLM agents. Current LLM agents often generate verbose textual reasoning at every decision step and allocate reasoning effort nearly uniformly across turns, leading to substantial inefficiency in multi-turn agentic trajectories. We propose Adaptive Latent Agentic Reasoning (ALAR), a dual-mode framework that uses compact latent reasoning for routine turns and selectively escalates to explicit chain-of-thought when deeper deliberation is needed. ALAR learns latent reasoning by using the agent's actions as supervision anchors and is further optimized to use latent reasoning when it is sufficient for task success and reserve explicit CoT for harder decisions. Experiments on agentic search and tool-use benchmarks show that ALAR maintains comparable or better task accuracy while substantially reducing generated tokens by up to 43.6% in search and 84.6% in tool use. These results demonstrate that ALAR improves the accuracy-efficiency trade-off of LLM agents by reducing unnecessary textual reasoning while preserving explicit deliberation for harder decision steps.

</details>


### [83] [WRIT: Write-Read Intensive Trajectory Synthesis for Multi-Turn User-Facing Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02908v1)
*Hengrui Gu,Xiaotian Han,Kaixiong Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出多轮agent训练轨迹合成方法WRIT，强调读写密集型任务，可迁移至coding agent的训练数据生成。

TL;DR: 提出WRIT方法，通过合成写-读密集型轨迹训练多轮代理，强调单个写入决策的证据负担，仅用2K轨迹训练4B模型在τ²基准上超越GPT-5.1 no-think且推理时token大幅减少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有写密集型轨迹数据无法应对需要大量阅读证据才能做出单个写入决策的困难情况。

Method: 沿写入决策数量和每个决策的证据负担两个维度合成轨迹，首先生成写密集型和读密集型任务，然后多样化用户行为指令，最后在可执行环境中模拟交互产生完整轨迹。

Result: 在τ²基准上，4B模型（WRIT训练）优于GPT-5.1 no-think，且推理时token使用量大幅减少。

Conclusion: 紧凑的SFT数据可将部分昂贵的测试时推理转化为高效的代理行为。

中文摘要：多轮面向用户的代理必须从不完整的请求中推断用户意图，通过对话和工具收集缺失信息，并执行有效操作。训练轨迹记录了这一过程，作为用户消息、代理响应、工具调用等的交错序列。合成足够复杂的轨迹已成为训练代理的主要途径：现有流程通常通过将多个用户请求组合成更长的任务来增加难度，产生写密集型轨迹，训练顺序执行。我们认为，当代理必须收集和比较大量读取工具的证据才能使其参数变得可识别时，单个写入决策本身可能很困难，这是写密集型数据单独无法解决的挑战。受此启发，我们提出了WRIT（写-读密集型轨迹合成），这是一个沿两个复杂性维度合成多轮代理训练轨迹的流程：任务中写入决策的数量和每个决策的证据负担。WRIT首先生成写密集型和读密集型任务。然后多样化用户行为指令以反映现实对话变化，最后在可执行环境中模拟代理-用户交互以产生完整的训练轨迹。由此产生的数据不仅训练代理执行更长的任务，而且在高信息负载下进行稳健的、基于证据的决策。仅使用2K合成轨迹，在WRIT上训练的4B模型在τ²基准上优于GPT-5.1 no-think，并大幅减少推理时token使用，表明紧凑的SFT数据可以将部分昂贵的测试时推理转化为高效的代理行为。

Original abstract: Multi-turn user-facing agents must infer user intent from incomplete requests, collect missing information through dialogue and tools, and execute valid actions. A training trajectory records this process as an interleaved sequence of user messages, agent responses, tool calls, etc. Synthesizing sufficiently complex trajectory has become a central route to train agents: existing pipelines often increase difficulty by composing multiple user requests into longer tasks, producing write-intensive trajectories that train sequential execution.
  We argue that a single write decision can itself be difficult when the agent must gather and compare substantial read-tool evidence before its arguments become identifiable, a challenge that write-intensive data alone cannot address. Guided by this insight, we propose WRIT (\uline{W}rite-\uline{R}ead \uline{I}ntensive \uline{T}rajectory Synthesis), a pipeline for synthesizing multi-turn agent training trajectories along two complexity axes: the number of write decisions in a task and the evidence burden of each individual decision. WRIT first generates write-intensive and read-heavy tasks. It then diversifies user behavior instructions to reflect realistic conversational variation, and finally simulates agent-user interactions in an executable environment to produce complete training trajectories. The resulting data trains agents not only for longer task execution, but also for robust, evidence-grounded decision making under high information load. With only 2K synthesized trajectories, a 4B model trained on WRIT outperforms GPT-5.1 no-think on $τ^2$-bench and substantially reduces inference-time token usage, showing that compact SFT data can convert part of expensive test-time reasoning into efficient agent behavior.

</details>

### [84] [Two-Fidelity Best-Action Identification for Stochastic Minimax Tree](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01708v1)
*Peter Chen,Xi Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 二保真度树搜索，可迁移至agent规划中的多保真度评估。

TL;DR: 提出2FFS算法，结合多保真思想在树搜索中自适应选择廉价或精确评估，理论保证正确性和有限停止，实验显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度极小极大搜索和MCTS中，启发式评估廉价但有偏，精确展开可靠但昂贵，需要一种平衡两者以降低总体成本的方法。

Method: 提出2FFS算法，融合极大极小快速扩展与MCTS随机采样，通过多保真赌博机决策机制自适应选择低保真（有偏）或高保真（精确）评估。

Result: 理论证明固定置信度下正确性、精确识别有限停止性及多项式深度成本上界；实验在随机树上相比BAI-MCTS基线显著减少样本和计算操作。

Conclusion: 2FFS有效解决了随机极大极小树中最佳动作识别问题，实现了成本与精度的平衡，具有理论和实践价值。

中文摘要：我们研究固定置信度下随机极大极小树的最佳动作识别（BAI）。这个问题在现代AI规划中越来越重要，其中深度极大极小搜索和蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）与语言模型长展开面临一个基本权衡：启发式评估廉价但有偏，而精确展开可靠但昂贵。我们提出2FFS，一种双保真树搜索算法，将多保真平坦赌博机思想引入树中。该算法结合了极大极小风格的快速扩展和MCTS风格的随机采样，自适应地决定何时利用廉价的带偏评估，何时调用昂贵的精确评估进行局部验证。我们证明了固定置信度正确性，建立了精确识别的有限停止性，并给出了通用深度树的深度多项式成本上界。在数值随机树实验中，与现有的BAI-MCTS基线相比，2FFS使用的样本和计算操作显著更少。

Original abstract: We study fixed-confidence best-action identification (BAI) in stochastic minimax trees. This problem is increasingly relevant in modern AI planning, where deep minimax search and Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) with language model long rollouts face a fundamental tradeoff: heuristic evaluations are cheap but biased, while accurate rollouts are reliable but prohibitively expensive. We propose 2FFS, a two-fidelity tree-search algorithm that brings multi-fidelity flat bandit ideas into trees. The algorithm combines minimax-style fast expansion with MCTS-style stochastic sampling, adaptively deciding when to exploit cheap biased evaluations and when to invoke expensive accurate evaluations for local certification. We prove fixed-confidence correctness, establish finite stopping for exact identification, and give a polynomial-depth cost upper bound for general-depth trees. Across numerical stochastic-tree experiments, 2FFS uses substantially fewer samples and computational operations comparing to existing BAI-MCTS baseline.

</details>


### [85] [Adaptive Auto-Harness: Sustained Self-Improvement for Agentic System Deployment on Open-Ended Task Streams](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01770v2)
*Zewen Liu,Zhan Shi,Yisi Sang,Bing He,Minhua Lin,Tianxin Wei,Dakuo Wang,Benoit Dumoulin,Wei Jin,Hanqing Lu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 自适应自动harness框架，直接实现agent自我改进与任务流适应。

TL;DR: 提出了自适应自动工具框架，通过分解演化损失和适应损失、使用多智能体演化器和工具树路由，在开放式任务流中持续优化LLM代理，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动工具系统在固定离线基准上表现良好，但实际部署中遇到任务流开放、异构和分布漂移等挑战，导致单一密集更新的工具脆性并性能下降。

Method: 将到预言工具的差距分解为演化损失和适应损失，采用有状态多智能体演化器、工具树解时路由和人工引导钩子来分别解决两类损失。

Result: 在预测市场、安全竞赛和事件预测三个流上，自适应自动工具优于五个基线，消融实验验证了构建、路由和人工引导各组件贡献。

Conclusion: 自适应自动工具框架能有效处理开放式任务流中的持续工具构建，通过任务自适应和综合优化提升LLM代理性能。

中文摘要：自动工具系统如A-Evolve、GEPA和Meta-Harness通过从执行反馈优化提示、技能、工具、记忆和支持基础设施来改进LLM代理，但它们通常是在固定的离线基准上进行评估。实际部署呈现的是开放式的任务流：历史记录增长没有固定终点，异构任务需要不同的工具，问题分布随时间变化。这些挑战使得一个单一、反复密集更新的工具变得脆弱，导致性能退化，表现为准确率早期达到峰值然后下降。这激发了具有任务自适应性的持续工具构建。我们引入了自适应自动工具（Adaptive Auto-Harness），一个针对此类流的框架和系统。该框架将到预言工具（oracle harness）的差距分解为演化损失和适应损失。该系统通过有状态的多智能体演化器、具有解时路由的工具树以及在历史缺乏所需信号时的人工引导钩子来解决这些损失。在预测市场、安全竞赛和事件预测流中，自适应自动工具优于五个现有的自动工具基线，消融实验将收益归因于更好的构建、路由或定向人工引导。代码可在https://github.com/A-EVO-Lab/a-evolve/tree/release/adaptive-auto-harness获取。

Original abstract: Auto-harness systems such as A-Evolve, GEPA, and Meta-Harness improve LLM agents by optimizing prompts, skills, tools, memories, and supporting infrastructure from execution feedback, but they are typically evaluated on fixed offline benchmarks. Real deployments instead present open-ended task streams: histories grow without a fixed endpoint, heterogeneous tasks require different harnesses, and problem distributions shift over time. These challenges make a single repeatedly and densely updated harness brittle, causing performance degradation as accuracy peaks early and then declines. This motivates sustained harness construction with task-wise adaptation. We introduce Adaptive Auto-Harness, a framework and system for such streams. The framework decomposes the gap to an oracle harness into evolution loss and adaptation loss. The system addresses these losses with a stateful multi-agent evolver, a harness tree with solve-time routing, and human-steering hooks for cases where history lacks the needed signal. Across prediction-market, security-competition, and event-forecasting streams, Adaptive Auto-Harness outperforms five existing auto-harness baselines and ablations attribute gains to better construction, routing, or targeted human steering. Code is available in \href{https://github.com/A-EVO-Lab/a-evolve/tree/release/adaptive-auto-harness}{Link}.

</details>


### [86] [OpenWebRL: Demystifying Online Multi-turn Reinforcement Learning for Visual Web Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02031v2)
*Rui Yang,Qianhui Wu,Yuxi Chen,Hao Bai,Wenlin Yao,Hao Cheng,Baolin Peng,Huan Zhang,Tong Zhang,Jianfeng Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 开源视觉web agent在线多轮RL训练框架，系统研究设计选择，可迁移至coding agent训练。

TL;DR: 提出OpenWebRL框架，用在线多轮RL在真实网站上训练视觉网络代理，仅用少量数据就达到开源SOTA，并可与专有系统竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源视觉网络代理依赖大量人工收集的演示数据，可扩展性差；在线RL在文本代理中有效，但在视觉网络代理中未充分探索。

Method: 构建OpenWebRL框架，包括实时浏览器基础设施、监督初始化、多模态上下文管理、轨迹级成功判断和多轮策略优化，利用在线RL在真实网站上训练。

Result: OpenWebRL-4B在Online-Mind2Web和DeepShop上分别达到67.0%和64.0%成功率，超越同类开源代理，与专有系统竞争。

Conclusion: 在线RL可以高效训练视觉网络代理，提供了一条构建强大、可复现、低成本开源代理的实用路径。

中文摘要：构建能够胜任的视觉网络代理需要长程推理、精确定位以及与动态真实网站的稳健交互。尽管进展迅速，最强的系统仍主要来自专有领域，而开源代理仍然严重依赖于对大量策划的网络轨迹进行监督后训练。这种依赖造成了重大的可扩展性瓶颈：高质量的演示收集成本高昂，而静态数据集对多样且不断变化的开放网络覆盖有限。尽管在线RL在基于文本的代理中显示出前景，但其直接在实时网站上训练视觉网络代理的潜力在很大程度上仍未被探索。在本文中，我们介绍了OpenWebRL，一个用于在真实网站上通过在线多轮RL训练视觉网络代理的开放框架。OpenWebRL涵盖了完整的训练流程，包括可扩展的实时浏览器基础设施、监督初始化、多模态上下文管理、轨迹级成功判断以及高效的多轮策略优化。利用该框架，我们训练了OpenWebRL-4B，其在具有挑战性的实时网络基准上确立了新的开源最优水平。仅使用0.4K初始化轨迹和2.2K开放式RL训练任务，OpenWebRL-4B在Online-Mind2Web上达到67.0%的成功率，在DeepShop上达到64.0%，优于先前类似或更大规模的开源代理，并与包括OpenAI CUA和Gemini CUA在内的专有系统保持竞争力。除了强大的基准性能外，我们系统地研究了使在线RL对视觉网络代理有效的关键设计选择，并分析了RL如何改进代理推理。总体而言，我们的工作为构建更强大、可复现且成本效益更高的开源网络代理提供了一条实用路径。我们将发布我们的训练数据、模型和代码以支持未来的研究。

Original abstract: Building capable visual web agents requires long-horizon reasoning, precise grounding, and robust interaction with dynamic real-world websites. Despite rapid progress, the strongest systems remain largely proprietary, while open agents still depend heavily on supervised post-training over large collections of curated web trajectories. This dependence creates a major scalability bottleneck: high-quality demonstrations are expensive to collect, and static datasets offer limited coverage of the diverse, ever-changing open web. Although online RL has shown promise for text-based agents, its potential for training visual web agents directly on live websites remains largely underexplored. In this paper, we introduce OpenWebRL, an open framework for training visual web agents with online multi-turn RL on real websites. OpenWebRL covers the full training pipeline, including scalable live-browser infrastructure, supervised initialization, multimodal context management, trajectory-level success judging, and efficient multi-turn policy optimization. Using this framework, we train OpenWebRL-4B, which establishes a new open-source state of the art on challenging live-web benchmarks. With only 0.4K initialization trajectories and 2.2K open-ended RL training tasks, OpenWebRL-4B achieves 67.0% success on Online-Mind2Web and 64.0% on DeepShop, outperforming prior open agents of similar or larger scale and remaining competitive with proprietary systems including OpenAI CUA and Gemini CUA. Beyond strong benchmark performance, we systematically study the key design choices that make online RL effective for visual web agents, and analyze how RL improves agentic reasoning. Overall, our work offers a practical path toward building more capable, reproducible, and cost-efficient open web agents. We will release our training data, models, and code to support future research.

</details>


### [87] [Policy and World Modeling Co-Training for Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02388v1)
*Ning Lu,Baijiong Lin,Shengcai Liu,Jiahao Wu,Haoze Lv,Yanbin Wei,Lingting Zhu,Shengju Qian,Xin Wang,Ying-Cong Chen,Qi Wang,Ke Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 利用RL rollout进行policy和world model共训练，通用agent训练方法。

TL;DR: PaW通过强化学习中的策略展开数据，在不改变推理方式的情况下，为语言智能体提供世界建模辅助监督，显著提升了性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习只关注动作的奖励，缺乏对动作环境影响的监督，而世界建模可弥补此不足，但现有方法代价高；我们观察到RL展开本身包含动作与下一观察的配对，可用于世界建模。

Method: 提出PaW框架，在RL训练中同时进行策略和世界建模的协同训练，包括三个组件：基于动作熵选择WM数据、噪声容忍WM损失、奖励自适应损失平衡。

Result: 在三个智能体任务基准上，PaW在不同模型和RL算法下均持续优于强RL基线。

Conclusion: 标准RL展开是语言智能体训练中世界建模监督的实用来源，PaW框架有效结合了RL和WM的优势。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）通过教导大型语言模型（LLM）智能体哪些动作能带来高奖励来改进它们，但很少监督这些动作对环境的影响。世界建模（WM）可以填补这一空白，然而现有方法通常需要单独的模拟器、额外的训练阶段或额外的推理时间计算。我们观察到，在策略RL的展开已经包含了所需的信号：每个转移将动作与其产生的下一观察配对。基于这一观察，我们提出了PaW，一种策略与世界建模协同训练框架，在不改变推理范式的情况下，在RL过程中向同一策略添加辅助的世界建模监督。为了使辅助的世界建模监督信息丰富且稳定，PaW引入了三个组件：基于动作熵的WM数据选择、容忍噪声的WM损失和奖励自适应损失平衡。在三个智能体任务基准上的实验表明，在不同模型和RL算法上，PaW均优于强RL基线。这些结果表明，标准RL展开是语言智能体训练中WM监督的实用来源。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) improves large language model (LLM) agents by teaching them which actions lead to high rewards, but provides little supervision on what those actions do to the environment. World modeling (WM) can fill this gap, yet existing approaches often require separate simulators, extra training stages, or additional inference-time computation. We observe that on-policy RL rollouts already contain the needed signal: each transition pairs an action with its resulting next observation. Based on this observation, we propose PaW, a Policy and World modeling co-training framework that adds auxiliary WM supervision to the same policy during RL, without changing the inference paradigm. To make auxiliary WM supervision informative and stable, PaW introduces three components: action-entropy-based WM data selection, noise-tolerant WM loss, and reward-adaptive loss balancing. Experiments on three agentic task benchmarks show consistent improvements over strong RL baselines across models and RL algorithms. These results suggest that standard RL rollouts are a practical source of WM supervision for language-agent training.

### [88] [Filter, Then Reweight: Rethinking Optimization Granularity in On-Policy Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02684v2)
*Yuying Li,Leqi Zheng,Yongzi Yu,Wenrui Zhou,Xuchang Zhong,Xing Hu,Jing Jin,Hangjie Yuan,Tao Feng*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出轨迹级和token级过滤重加权方法，可迁移至agent训练中的轨迹选择与优化。

TL;DR: 提出FiRe-OPD方法，通过轨迹过滤和标记软加权实现更细粒度的同策略蒸馏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有同策略蒸馏方法在优化粒度上存在不足，需要同时考虑轨迹和标记级别的选择性训练。

Method: FiRe-OPD首先过滤低质量轨迹，然后对保留轨迹内的标记进行软重新加权以强调信息丰富的标记。

Result: 在强到弱、单教师和多教师设置中，FiRe-OPD优于近期标记级方法，例如在AIME 2024上提升6.25分，在Miner上提升18.81分。

Conclusion: FiRe-OPD通过软加权机制有效缓解信息损失并增强优化稳定性，实现更细粒度的同策略蒸馏优化。

中文摘要：在大型语言模型中，同策略蒸馏正从全轨迹KL监督转向更具选择性的训练范式。最近的同策略蒸馏方法越来越关注选择哪些轨迹进行学习、哪些标记最具信息量以及哪些监督信号最可靠。受这一趋势启发，我们重新思考同策略蒸馏的优化粒度，并提出FiRe-OPD（过滤，然后重新加权），它在轨迹和标记两个层面联合调整监督信号。具体来说，FiRe-OPD首先过滤轨迹以移除低质量的 rollout 样本，然后在保留的轨迹内应用软重新加权以强调信息丰富的标记。与硬性标记选择相比，FiRe-OPD利用软加权机制有效缓解信息损失并增强优化稳定性，从而实现更细粒度的同策略蒸馏优化。我们在强到弱、单教师和多教师设置中验证了FiRe-OPD的有效性，并展示了其相对于近期标记级同策略蒸馏方法的优越性（例如，在强到弱设置中AIME 2024上+6.25，在多教师设置中Miner上+18.81）。我们的代码可在https://github.com/YuYingLi0/FiRe-OPD获取。

Original abstract: On-Policy distillation (OPD) in large language models is shifting from full-trace KL supervision toward more selective training paradigms. Recent OPD methods increasingly focus on selecting which trajectories to learn from, which tokens are most informative, and which supervision signals are most reliable. Motivated by this trend, we rethink optimization granularity of OPD and propose \fireicon\ FiRe-OPD (Filter, then Reweight), which jointly adjusts supervision signals at both trajectory and token levels. In details, FiRe-OPD first filters trajectories to remove low-quality rollout samples, and then applies soft reweighting within the retained trajectories to emphasize informative tokens. Compared with hard token selection, FiRe-OPD leverages a soft-weighting mechanism to effectively mitigate information loss and enhance optimization stability, thereby achieving finer-grained OPD optimization. We validate the effectiveness of FiRe-OPD across strong-to-weak, single-teacher, and multi-teacher settings, and demonstrate its superiority over recent token-level OPD methods ( (e.g., +6.25 on AIME 2024 in strong-to-weak, +18.81 on Miner in multi-teacher). Our code is available at https://github.com/YuYingLi0/FiRe-OPD.

</details>


### [89] [Position: Deployed Reinforcement Learning should be Continual](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04029v2)
*Parnian Behdin,Kevin Roice,Golnaz Mesbahi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出持续RL观点，可迁移至agent持续学习

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作为立场论文，本文通过理论论证识别了部署后智能体面临的四个非平稳性来源，并分析了现实世界中持续RL的成功案例，从而提出转向持续学习的建议。

Result: 识别了四个导致非平稳性的来源，并展示了持续学习在现实世界中的成功应用，证明了持续学习的必要性。

Conclusion: 社区应放弃“训练-再修复”范式，采用持续学习范式，以实现自适应和长期优化的部署智能体。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）在现实世界用例中受到越来越多的关注和采用。大多数这些系统遵循“训练-再修复”范式，其中训练好的智能体在与世界交互时不学习，直到性能下降并且需要重新训练。在这篇立场论文中，我们认为部署一个无法达到最优但接收评估性奖励信号的智能体，本质上是一个持续学习问题。我们确定了部署后需要永无止境学习的四个非平稳性来源，并强调了为什么最好的已部署智能体从不停止适应。我们分析了现实世界中持续学习成功案例，并向社区展示了摆脱当前“训练-再修复”范式的优势和措施。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has received increasing attention and adoption in real-world use cases. Most of these systems follow a train-then-fix paradigm, where trained agents do not learn while interacting with the world until performance degrades and retraining becomes necessary. In this position paper, we argue that deploying an agent that is incapable of optimality, but receives an evaluative reward signal, is inherently a continual RL problem. We identify four sources of non-stationarity after deployment that necessitate never-ending learning, and highlight why the best deployed agents never stop adapting. We analyze successful examples of continual RL in the real world, and present the community with the advantages and measures to move away from the current train-then-fix paradigm.

### [90] [Forgetting is Not Erasure: Recovering Latent Knowledge via Transport Keys](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02860v1)
*Archie Chaudhury*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究遗忘恢复，对agent记忆管理有启发

TL;DR: 本文发现灾难性遗忘主要由接口漂移而非计算擦除引起，通过传输键可恢复大部分遗忘性能，表明持续学习需要更好的计算索引机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战灾难性遗忘是表征擦除的传统观点，探索遗忘的机制本质。

Method: 提出拼接评估协议和传输键（紧凑接口对齐算子）来分离接口漂移与计算擦除的影响。

Result: 在分割CIFAR-100上，传输键恢复了ResNet和ViT中大部分顺序学习后的性能。

Conclusion: 持续学习应关注计算索引和重访问，而非仅限制权重更新。

中文摘要：灾难性遗忘通常被视为一个表征问题：在顺序训练后，模型似乎丢失了支持早期任务的特征。我们挑战了这一观点的更强形式。在受控的持续学习环境中，我们发现很大一部分明显的遗忘可以归因于内部阶段之间的接口漂移，而不是任务相关计算的永久擦除。我们通过一种拼接评估协议来研究这一现象，该协议将更新后网络的早期计算与其前身的后期计算相结合，并可选地通过一个紧凑的、特定任务的传输键进行中介。我们从系统层面将传输键描述为紧凑的接口对齐算子，这些算子从一小对配对的锚点激活中估计，并通过模型拼接进行评估。在分割CIFAR-100上使用ResNet风格网络时，传输键在顺序训练任务B后恢复了大部分原始任务A的性能。在紧凑视觉Transformer上，我们观察到类似的恢复模式。这些结果表明，持续学习可能需要更好的机制来索引和重新访问潜在计算，而不仅仅是防止权重变化的方法。

Original abstract: Catastrophic forgetting is often framed as a representational problem: after sequential training, a model appears to lose the features that supported performance on earlier tasks. We challenge the stronger form of this view. Across controlled continual-learning settings, we find that a significant portion of apparent forgetting can be attributed to interface drift between internal stages rather than permanent erasure of task-relevant computation. We study this phenomenon through a stitched evaluation protocol that combines early computation from a post-update network with late computation from its predecessor, optionally mediated by a compact, task-specific transport key. We describe transport keys at a systems level as compact interface-alignment operators estimated from a small set of paired anchor activations and evaluated through model stitching. On split CIFAR-100 with a ResNet-style network, transport keys recover most of the original Task A performance after sequential training on Task B. On a compact vision transformer, we observe a similar recovery pattern. These results suggest that continual learning may require better mechanisms for indexing and re-accessing latent computations, not only methods that prevent weight change.

</details>

### [91] [TechRAG: Evidence-Gated Multimodal Agentic RAG for Technical Literature Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01613v2)
*Kanwar Bharat Singh*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 多智能体RAG框架，包含规划、检索、验证等组件，属于通用agent推理方法。

TL;DR: 提出一个多模态智能体RAG框架，结合文本、图谱和视觉证据，用于特定领域文献推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统单次RAG系统在领域特定文献推理中证据不足，需要更自主、多模态的检索与生成架构。

Method: 采用证据门控流水线，包括查询意图分类、文本和视觉查询改写、FAISS/BM25混合检索与交叉编码器重排序、Neo4j图谱引导块遍历、ColSmol视觉检索与MaxSim重排序、100分制证据评分与重试机制、外部学术数据库搜索、多智能体生成（规划者、研究者、写作者、批评者）及自修正。

Result: 实现了可扩展的多模态检索架构（4万页文档），具备证据充分性评估、多智能体生成和知识图谱支持，提升了领域文献推理的实用性和准确性。

Conclusion: 该框架为专门研究语料库上的技术推理提供了实用的、证据门控的多模态智能体RAG解决方案。

中文摘要：本文提出了一种面向特定领域文献推理的智能多模态检索增强生成（RAG）框架，并在一个包含数千篇关于智能轮胎、车辆动力学、车辆控制、感知、估计和机器学习等领域论文的精选语料库上进行了实例化。与传统的单次RAG系统不同，所提出的架构采用自主的、证据门控的流水线，该流水线对查询意图进行分类，生成单独的文本和视觉查询改写，使用FAISS和BM25进行混合文本检索，随后进行交叉编码器重排序，通过Neo4j知识图谱上的图引导块遍历扩展证据，并使用ColSmol延迟交互嵌入与MUVERA固定维度编码、近似最近邻搜索和MaxSim重排序来检索视觉文档证据。该框架使用混合基于规则/LLM审查的100分制评分标准对证据充分性进行评分，通过带有漂移保护的重新表述进行重试检索，通过优化-搜索-验证循环搜索外部学术数据库，合并和去重多模态证据，验证引文完整性，并通过规划者、研究者、写作者和批评者智能体生成带引文的答案，并带有自我修正修订。主要贡献包括：（i）一种可扩展的多模态检索架构，结合了超过40,000页文档的文本、图谱和视觉证据；（ii）一种可解释的证据充分性和重试机制；（iii）一个具有证据映射和批评者驱动修订的多智能体生成流水线；（iv）一个包含基于LLM的实体提取、OpenAlex作者验证和语料库内引文解析的领域知识图谱；（v）一种面向目标文献扩展的路径依赖外部搜索架构。结果是一个实用的、证据门控的、多模态智能体RAG架构，用于专门研究语料库上的技术推理。

Original abstract: This paper presents an agentic multimodal retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) framework for domain-specific literature reasoning, instantiated on a curated corpus of several thousand papers in intelligent tires, vehicle dynamics, vehicle control, sensing, estimation, and machine learning. Unlike conventional single-pass RAG systems, the proposed architecture uses an autonomous, evidence-gated pipeline that classifies query intent, generates separate text and visual query rewrites, performs hybrid text retrieval with FAISS and BM25 followed by cross-encoder reranking, expands evidence through graph-guided chunk traversal over a Neo4j knowledge graph, and retrieves visual document evidence using ColSmol late-interaction embeddings with MUVERA fixed-dimensional encoding, approximate nearest-neighbor search, and MaxSim reranking. The framework scores evidence sufficiency using a 100-point rubric with hybrid rule-based/LLM review, retries retrieval through drift-guarded reformulation, searches external academic databases through optimize--search--vet loops, merges and deduplicates multimodal evidence, verifies citation integrity, and generates cited answers through Planner, Researcher, Writer, and Critic agents with self-correcting revision. Key contributions include: (i) a scalable multimodal retrieval architecture combining text, graph, and visual evidence over 40,000 document pages; (ii) an interpretable evidence sufficiency and retry mechanism; (iii) a multi-agent generation pipeline with evidence mapping and critic-driven revision; (iv) a domain knowledge graph with LLM-based entity extraction, OpenAlex author validation, and intra-corpus citation resolution; and (v) a route-dependent external search architecture for targeted literature expansion. The result is a practical, evidence-gated, multimodal agentic RAG architecture for technical reasoning over specialized research corpora.

</details>


### [92] [ODTQA-FoRe: An Open-Domain Tabular Question Answering Dataset for Future Data Forecasting and Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02433v1)
*Zhensheng Wang,Xiaole Liu,Wenmian Yang,Kun Zhou,Yiquan Zhang,Weijia Jia*

Main category: cs.IR

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 大量实验证明了TimeFore的有效性。

Conclusion: TimeFore框架通过协作角色有效解决了LLM在时间序列预测和复杂推理上的局限性，为开放域表格问答的未来预测任务提供了可行方案。

中文摘要：LLM的快速发展显著推进了表格问答，但大多数系统无法进行面向未来的数值预测。为解决这一空白，我们引入了一个新任务——面向未来数据预测与推理的开放域表格问答，并提出了首个使用房地产数据覆盖时间序列预测和基于预测推理场景的数据集。该任务在检索精确历史数据、克服LLM的预测限制以及标准化多样化查询响应方面提出了挑战。为解决上述挑战，我们提出了TimeFore，一个基于LLM代理的框架，将问题分解为三个协作角色：检索器自主生成SQL以获取数据，预测器调用外部时间序列模型以提高准确性，分析器综合结果以构建精确且一致的最终答案。大量实验证明了我们TimeFore的有效性。

Original abstract: The rapid development of LLMs has significantly advanced tabular question answering, but most systems cannot perform future-oriented numerical prediction. To address this gap, we introduce a novel task, Open-Domain Tabular Question Answering for Future Data Forecasting and Reasoning, and propose the first dataset to cover time-series forecasting and forecast-based reasoning scenarios using real estate data. This task poses challenges in retrieving precise historical data, overcoming the forecasting limitations of LLMs, and standardizing responses for diverse queries. To solve the above challenges, we propose TimeFore, an LLM agent-based framework that decomposes the problem into three collaborative roles: a Retriever autonomously generates SQL to fetch data, a Forecaster invokes external time-series models for higher accuracy, and an Analyzer synthesizes the results to construct a precise and consistent final answer. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of our TimeFore.

</details>


### [93] [The Crowded Embedding Space: A Mean-Field Mechanism for Emergent Marginalization in Retrieval-Augmented Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28343v1)
*Shwan Ashrafi,Dan Roth*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 分析检索增强agent的嵌入空间问题，对agent检索设计有启发

TL;DR: 检索增强智能体中，多数兴趣的高密度文档会几何挤占少数兴趣的检索结果，导致性能崩溃和公平性问题，且局部相关性目标会使系统自组织为仅服务多数兴趣的状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前检索增强生成智能体按查询独立评估，忽略了嵌入空间中几何耦合的交互，导致多数兴趣挤占少数兴趣的检索结果，产生公平性问题。

Method: 建立形式化框架，进行静态分析揭示相变现象，并推导非线性福克-普朗克方程分析动态演化。

Result: 静态下多数目标密度增加导致少数目标性能灾难性崩溃；动态下局部相关性目标触发全局机制系统性地边缘化少数兴趣，使系统自组织为仅服务多数兴趣的状态。

Conclusion: 检索增强智能体中的局部相关性目标会导致空间拥挤，从而系统性地损害少数用户利益，这是其关键基础支撑失败模式。

中文摘要：检索增强的生成式智能体依赖于检索来进行基础支撑，但通常是在逐个查询的基础上进行评估。这割裂了在共享嵌入空间中几何耦合的交互。例如，我们表明，为了满足多数兴趣（例如，通用的“犯罪”电影）所需的高文档密度可能会在几何上挤占语义相似的少数兴趣（例如，“黑色电影”）的检索邻域，从而有效地将少数内容从top-$k$结果中排除。我们引入了一个形式化框架来分析密集检索中这种目标冲突如何引发固有的性能限制和新出现的公平性问题，这些问题源于空间拥挤。在我们的静态分析中，我们证明，对于固定的嵌入空间，当多数目标的密度增加时，会发生相变，少数用户目标的性能会灾难性地崩溃。然后，我们将此扩展到动态模型，并推导出一个非线性福克-普朗克方程，该方程支配着智能体为了最大化检索准确性而更新文档嵌入时的演化。我们的分析表明，这种局部相关性目标触发了一种新兴的全局机制，系统地边缘化了少数兴趣。我们证明，这些目标将驱使系统自组织成一个专门服务于多数兴趣的状态。这些结果为理解检索增强智能体中的一个关键基础支撑失败模式提供了理论基础。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generative agents rely on retrieval for grounding, yet are typically evaluated on a query-by-query basis. This isolates interactions that are geometrically coupled in a shared embedding space. For example, we show that the high document density required to serve majority interests (e.g., generic "Crime" movies) can geometrically overcrowd the retrieval neighborhood of a semantically similar minority (e.g., "Film Noir"), effectively expelling minority content from top-$k$ results. We introduce a formal framework to analyze how such goal collisions in dense retrieval induce fundamental performance limits and emergent fairness issues inherent to spatial crowding. In our static analysis, we demonstrate that for a fixed embedding space, a phase transition occurs where minority user goals suffer a catastrophic collapse in performance as the density of majority goals increases. We then extend this to a dynamic model and derive a non-linear Fokker-Planck equation that governs the evolution of document embeddings as the agent updates them to maximize retrieval accuracy. Our analysis reveals that this local relevance objective triggers an emergent global mechanism that systematically marginalizes minority interests. We prove that such objectives drive the system to self-organize into a state that exclusively serves majority interests. These results provide a theoretical foundation for understanding a critical grounding failure mode in retrieval-augmented agents.

</details>


### [94] [PIXELRAG: Web Screenshots Beat Text for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28344v1)
*Yichuan Wang,Zhifei Li,Zirui Wang,Paul Teiletche,Lesheng Jin,Matei Zaharia,Joseph E. Gonzalez,Sewon Min*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 基于截图的检索增强方法PixelRAG，可作为agent检索模块的通用组件，对代码检索有潜在启发。

TL;DR: PixelRAG通过直接使用网页截图进行检索和阅读，在多种任务上超越文本RAG，并实现3倍token压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于文本的网络检索方法丢弃了布局、视觉结构等丰富信息，而网页本质是视觉的，因此提出直接在像素空间进行检索和阅读的方法。

Method: 采用视觉嵌入模型（Qwen3-VL-Embedding）对网页截图编码，通过对比学习微调；检索后直接将截图作为像素输入VLM，无需文本转换。

Result: 在NQ、SimpleQA、MMSearch、LiveVQA、MoNaCo等基准上准确率提升最高达18.1%，并通过图像压缩实现3倍token成本降低。

Conclusion: 像素级RAG在性能和效率上优于文本RAG，挑战了网络检索中文本表示的必要性。

中文摘要：通过检索网络文本来增强大型语言模型（LLM）已成为主导范式，然而网络本质上并非文本形式：现有系统依赖于复杂的解析流水线，将HTML线性化并丢弃布局、视觉结构和格式。我们提出了PixelRAG，一种新的检索增强方法，它以原生的视觉形式表示网站，并完全在像素空间中进行检索和阅读，实现了消除文本抽象的端到端架构。据我们所知，PixelRAG是首个以这种形式对整个维基百科语料库进行操作的流水线，通过高效的视觉检索索引扩展到了3000万张截图图像的数据存储。基于现有的视觉嵌入模型（即Qwen3-VL-Embedding），PixelRAG进一步在截图数据上进行了微调，使用了精心策划的对比训练数据。检索到的截图直接作为像素输入馈送到视觉语言模型（VLM），无需中间文本转换。PixelRAG在无检索和基于文本的RAG基线上持续取得更好性能，最令人惊讶的是在广泛研究的文本中心任务（如NQ和SimpleQA）上。它还在多模态开放域问答（如MMSearch）、嘈杂新闻语料库基准（如LiveVQA）和智能体基准（如MoNaCo）上取得了显著提升，相比基于文本的基线准确率提高了高达18.1%。最后，像素表示通过图像压缩为RAG提供了新的效率杠杆，在较低分辨率下实现了高达3倍的token成本降低，同时保持了准确率。我们的结果挑战了网络检索中文本表示的必要性，表明网络RAG可以直接以网络原生的视觉形式运行，同时提高性能和效率。

Original abstract: Augmenting large language models (LLMs) with retrieved web text has become a dominant paradigm, yet the web is not natively textual: existing systems depend on complex parsing pipelines that linearize HTML and discard layout, visual structure, and formatting. We introduce PixelRAG, a new retrieval-augmented method that represents websites in their native visual form and performs retrieval and reading entirely in pixel space, enabling an end-to-end architecture that eliminates text abstraction. PixelRAG is, to our knowledge, the first pipeline to operate over a full Wikipedia corpus in this form, scaling to a datastore of 30 million screenshot images with an efficient visual retrieval index. Built on an existing visual embedding model (i.e., Qwen3-VL-Embedding), PixelRAG further fine-tunes this model on screenshot data with carefully curated contrastive training data. Retrieved screenshots are then fed directly as pixel inputs to a VLM, without intermediate text conversion. PixelRAG consistently outperforms both no-retrieval and text-based RAG baselines, most surprisingly on widely studied text-centric tasks such as NQ and SimpleQA. It also achieves strong gains on multimodal open-domain QA (e.g., MMSearch), benchmarks over noisy news corpora (e.g., LiveVQA), and agentic benchmarks (e.g., MoNaCo), improving accuracy by up to 18.1% over text-based baselines. Finally, pixel representations enable a new efficiency lever for RAG through image compression, achieving up to 3x token cost reduction at lower resolutions while maintaining accuracy. Our results challenge the necessity of text representations in web retrieval, suggesting that web RAG can operate directly in the web's native visual form while improving both performance and efficiency.

</details>
